<<0010>> vijñāpanam |
va
1 kandogānāṃ yajñavidhiprasiddhyarthaṃ lāyāyaṇācāryeṇa ṛṣṭau hi
- hyaṇgranthāḥ prauढ़ brāhmaṇamādimam | ṣaḍū viṃśākhya dvitīyaṃ
syāttataḥ sāmavidhirbhavet | saṃhitopaniṣadaṃśo granthā aṣṭāvito-
ritā ityetenokeṣu māmavedoyeṣu sarveṣu brāhmaṇeṣu vihitānāṃ
mantrāṇāṃ parasparavirodhādidoṣaparihārārthañcaitāni sūtrāṇi vira-
citani | etānyeva śrotavāṇi kalpasūtrāṇīti ca kathyante |
bhikhāminācāryeteṣāṃ sūtrāṇāṃ bhāvyaṃ viracitam | asmin
nthe daśasaṃkhyākāḥ prapāṭhakābhidheyāḥ paricchedā varttante, prapāṭhakāśca
kaṇḍikābhirvibhaktāḥ, tenaiteṣāṃ prapāṭhakānāmadhye prathama dvitīya
punaḥ va caturtha pañcama ṣaṣṭhāṣṭama navameṣu dvādaśaśaḥ kaṇḍikāḥ santi
tṛtīsa tu trayodaśasaṃkhyakā daśame viṃśatisaṃkhyakāñca dṛśyante,
saptameyaṃ grantha ekonatriṃśādhikaśatasaṃkhyakaiḥ kaṇḍikābhiranvito
tenāte |
va tatra prathamaprapāṭhake tāvat paribhāṣāyā ūrddha ṛtviga yājya-
lakṣaṇādyanantaraṃ vṛtapratimantraṇādi pūtabhṛdāhavanīyādhikārānta
uktaḥ | dvitīye stomayogādi mārvakratukasāmānyavidhānāntaḥ |
ṭatauye ṣoड़śino guṇavidhānādi vāṇāvayavadravyavidhānāntaḥ |
caturye vāṇavayavācchādanadravyavidhānādi vājibhakṣaṇamantrāntaḥ |
pañcame cāturmāsyādhikāre varuṇapradhāsikabrahmatvakathanādi soma-

<<0011>> camasorbhakṣaṇāntaḥ | ṣaṣṭhe santaninaḥ sāmavidhānādi dyacaraprati
hārāntaḥ | saptame caturacarapratihārādi hoturājye gā yatrogā
nāntaḥ | aṣṭame ekāha-ahona-matrākhya kāṇḍavitayānvitayajña
pratikāṇḍe pṛthaga vidhividhānādi vājapeyavidhānāntaḥ | na
rājasūyavidhānādi ahīnavidhividhānāntaḥ | daśame savādhika
tatparibhāṣāvidhānādi saṃvatsaravidhānāntaḥ prastāvo niru-
pito’sti |
kasmin kāle lāyāyaṇācārya: prādurabhūt kadā vā etāni
svāṇi tena viracitāni tannirṇayaḥ kutrāpi na dṛśyate, vintu
kaiściddiddabhirvikramādityasya sārddhaśatavarṣapūrvāvadhi sūtraracanavāla
ityanumoyate, tadanumānasthāpi samocīnatvena pramāṇaṃ nāti |
pūrvasmin kāle yadā akṣararacanaṃ lipikāryya vā nābhūta
gurumukhāt śravaṇena śivyaparamparāṇāṃ kaṇṭhe’bhyasto veda ā, tadā
tadānīmalyābhyāsena śrutavahuviṣayamanāyāsena śivyāṇāṃ sārasot,
mācāryyāḥ saṃkṣepatastadarthaṃ maṅgalayya alpākṣareṇa vaharthapratipaṇārtha-
kāni sūtrāṇi viracitavantaḥ, tena vinopadeśaṃ teṣāṃ tātpayyāda-
dhāraṇaṃ na sambhavatīti | ata ācāryaparamparayā upadeśaṃ prāheva-
vantaḥ śiṣyāsteṣāṃ prakṛtamarthamavadhārayanti | ye cānye vyutpattivalena
tattātyayāvadhāraṇaya pravṛttāste viparītamarthamudbhāvayanti | ataḥ
satrāṇāṃ gurupadeśamavaśyamapekṣaṇīyam |
lāvyāyaṇaśrautasūtrāṇaṃ sadṛśāni drāhmāyaṇācārthyaviracitāni
chandogānāmaparāṇi śrautasūtrāṇi varttante | teṣu prāyaśa eteṣāṃ

pāṭhāryādeḥ sosādṛśyo dṛśyate, yatra kuvacit kiñcinmāvaviśeṣo
vidyate tatra tatra tajjñāpanārthaṃ mayā sarveṣāṃ satrāṇaṃ nimmradeśe
pṛthaktayā drāhmāyaṇamatamuddhṛtam | tena lāyāyaṇācāryavira-
citaśrautasūtrebhyo drāhmāyaṇacāryakṛtaśrautasūtreṣu kiyān viśeṣo
varttate tadavagamaḥ sukaro bhaviṣyatīti | dhanvikṛtayā lāyā-
yaṇaśrautasṛvavṛttyā ceteṣāṃ śrautasūtrāṇāmavayavācaraśodhanañca mayā

prathamaḥ prapāṭhakaḥ |
atha prathamā kaṇḍikā |
kimidaṃ sūtraṃ nāmaśāstraṃ | kimarthamidamārabhyate | yajñavi-
dhiprasiddhaye | iha hi chāndogye dvividhovidhiḥ, anutrāhmaṇikaḥ
ṣaṭprāmāṇikañca | tatrānubrāhmaṇikaḥ, yajuṣākarmasu liṅgato-
vidhānamarthagrahaṇādityata ārabhya sādhāraṇa
guṇa vidhistu sarvatreti
yāvat | aparaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇairnivartyate | kāni punastāni
ṣaṭ pramāṇani | brāhmaṇa sūtra ārṣeyakalpa ṛksāmasamāmnāyo-
hopadeśāḥ | tatra brāhmaṇe jyotirdaśādau klṛptau | ṣaṣṭhādiṣu ca
turdhvadhyāyeṣu jyotiṣṭomaḥ klṛptaḥ trisaṃsthaḥ savikalpaḥ maprāya-
ścittaḥ, prajāpatirakāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyetyata śrārabhya |
tathā daśame dvādaśāhasya samastaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ | tathā ekādaśādiṣu

<<0015>> jādyāyanī ye
. [1.1.1]
|
pañcasu adhyāyeṣu stomāyujyate satriyebhyo harmya ityata ārabhya
daśānāmahāṃ stotravidhiḥ | tāvetau jyotiṣṭomadaśāho gavāmaya-
nādonāṃ sahasrasamvatsaraparyantānāṃ prakṛtibhṛtau | evañcaivameva mamā-
snāyaṃ grahovā ṛgyajuḥmāmnāñca samāmnāyaparipaṭhitānāṃ liṅgato-
’nuvidhānamanāramyakarmārthatāvyutpatteḥ | tadevaṃ siddhaye idamucyate |
nanu yajñavidhiprasiddhaye sūtrārambha ityetadanarthakaṃ, tasmā-
nārabdhavyaṃ | thārabdhavyaṃ prayojanaṃ vaktavyaṃ | uccate, śrārabdhavya-
meva | kasmāt, aspaṣṭā’niṣṭaparyudāma śeṣaviṣyeka vidhivikalpa samu-
caya niyamārthaṃ śāstrārambhaḥ | aspaṣṭānāntāvat tasya dvādaśa-
dokṣopamada iti donopasadorvibhāgasaṃśayaṃ viśinaṣṭi titra
upasada iti | aniṣṭaparyudāmaḥ, dakṣiṇāmīnaḥ pratiharatī-
ti sa vidhiḥ paryudasyate dakṣiṇapūrvamaṭamadeśamīkṣamāṇaḥ pratihartteti |
śeṣavidhiḥ, tantra jahyādaprokte’pi kariṣyāmīti viditvetyaprocamānena
gamyate | tathā ekavidhivikalpaḥ, paryenamatriśan grāmakāmo yaje-
teti śrutiḥ, iha ca kāmāntaraṃ kanyate, kañcidarthamarhanyo na
prāpnuyāt anṛvṛtāṃ prathamena yajeteti | tathā samuccayaḥ, atha
yatsaṅgavavelāyāṃ sa ādirityanena sāptavidhyaṃ darśayatā oṃṅkāra-
udgīthādau niyamitaḥ, ādiśabdeneoṅkāra uccate, rathantare
vāgityādeyamityanena vikalpe prāpte āha, samuccayatu nānārtha-
tvāditi prastāvaśānyathā hi vāgudgothāderoṅkāra iti | tathā
niyamavidhiḥ, viśvarūpāṇāṃ gānamanāramya vidhānātsarvatra prāptī satyāṃ
jyotiṣṭome niyamyate, tāmi nānyatra viśvarūpāmyo na cānyatra

śrautasūtraṃ |
viśvarūpā jyotiṣṭomā jyotiṣṭomāditi jyotiṣṭome viśvarūpāṇaṃ
gānantriyamyate | tadevamādyānāṃ vidhānānāṃ antareṇa sūtrārambhānna
middhiḥ | tasmādyaducyate ārabdhavyaṃ sṛtramiti tadyuktaṃ | evaṃ siddhe
sūtrārambheśrārabhyate |
atha vidhyavyapadeśe sarvakratvadhikāraḥ || 1 ||
tatra śāstrādau athetyayannipāta śrānantaryāpetomaṅgalārthaḥ pūrva-
prakṛtāpekṣādhikārārthaśceti | maṅgalārthastāvat atha pratigrahaṇe,
nāmati, maṅgalādimadhyāvasānāni hi śāstāṇi āyumantyeva vī-
rapuruṣāṇi bhavanti, śiṣyācāryayorttitāni prathante maṅgalaṃ | kiṃ puna-
rathaśabde maṅgalārthatvamiti cet | apraśnastāvat, yāvatā autpatti-
kastu śabdasyārthena sambandhaḥ | thāyannipātapaṭhitevyesvartheṣu padyate,
atha arthagrahaṇapraśvādhikārānantaryyapṛṣṭaprativacanamaṅgalārthapūjā carite-
sviti uktaṃ maṅgalārthatvaṃ | atha pūrvaprakṛtāpekṣatve kiṃ prayojanaṃ,
kāni cāsya pūrvaprakṛtānīti | uccate, apekṣitaṃ hi śāstreṇa
vaktavyaṃ bhavati, laghunopāyena tatsiddhaṃ bhavati | kathamapekṣata iti
cet, lokavedayorvṛttānte uttaratvena prayogāt | dṛśyate cā-
yamubhayorlokavedayorasminna the
prayujyamānaḥ | loke tāvat,
środanamapekṣya taṇḍulapākaḥ karttavyaḥ, paryeṣaṇasiddhānyeva manasi
kṛtvātha taṇḍulamātraṃ prati vaktavye klṛpta odana iti, atha śabdena
sarvasādhanasampadaṃ lṛptāṃ darśayati | tathā vede, parkādisimāntaṃ

savanaṃ chandāṃsyādiśan gāyatryaivānasavanamāpyāyanamiti | lokaḥ,
audumbarīmucchrayiṣyan, anvāhāryyapacanaṃ prati yamunāmavamṭathamabhyava-
yantīti| adhikārārthaḥ, khalvapi loke tāvaccucaye śolavate
• samyakṛtapādopasaṅgrahāya athāsmai śāstramārabhyate | tathā veda,
gavādonadhikṛtyāha, athaiṣa gauratheṣa āyurathaivopacitiriti |
eṃva mādyathaśabda svārthasambandhā lokavedapratyayāḥ | evaṃ jyoti-

marthe’thaśabda iti siddhaṃ |
5
vidhyavyapadeśe sarvakratvadhikāraḥ | vidheḥ śravyapadeśa iti
ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ kriyate | vidhīyate vidhānaṃ veti vidhiḥ | mahanmevāca
iti kariṣyan pratimantrayetetyetadādi vidhirvakṣyate | tadādyasya
vidheradhikārodraṣṭavyaḥ | śravyapadeśe, navyapadeśovyapadeśaḥ | ana-
dhikṛtya kañcitkratumupadiśyamāno vidhiḥ sarvatra bhavati | vyapa-
deśaḥ, agniṣṭutvāmgneyonigada ityetadādi vidhirvyapadeśaviṣaya-
sarvakratuṣu sarvaśabdo niravaśeṣavācī, krameṇa
sarvakratūnāmadhikāraḥ | adhikārovyāpāraḥ prasaṅga ityeko’rthaḥ |
eṣa padārthaḥ | atha samudāyārthaḥ | etaduktaṃ bhavati, anadhikṛtya
kañcitkratuṃ vidhirupadiśyamānaḥ sarvatra bhavatīti |
eva bhavati |
etrañcedidhiriti śakyamavakuṃ, kasmāt, nirdeśataḥ siddheḥ |
mahanme voca iti kariyan pratimantra yetetyetadādirnirdiśyata eva
vidhiḥ | śravyapadeśa ityetadapi na vaktavyaṃ, kasmāt, sāmānya-
viśeṣābhyāṃ vidhayo bhavanti | tatra sāmānyovidhirautsargikaḥ sarvatra

bhavati, atastasya viśeṣo’pavādaḥ | tatrāpavādenāviśeṣo bādhi-
ghyate, tasmācchakyamavaktu | sarvakravadhikāra ityatrāpi sarvagrahaṇaṃ
śakyamavatu, ṛtepi sarvagrahaṇa tprasaktamidamanyatra viśeṣagrahaṇāt |
adhikāraśabdoṣyatiricyata eva, kasmāt, uktamadhikārārthatvama-
thaśabdasyeti, sarvakratūna cikṛtyāyaśabda: pravarttate śāstrādāviti |
ataḥ sarvamidaṃ sūtraṃ nārabdhavyaṃ | athārabhyate prayojana vyaktavyaṃ |
nānārabdhavyaṃ, ārabdhayameva, kasmāt, anārambhe vidhirna sidhyeta |
tatra yattāvaducyate vidhigrahaṇaṃ na karttavyamityatra brūmaḥ | kartta-
vyameva | kimarthaṃ śeṣavidhyupasaṅgrahārthaṃ, yepi vidhayona parāṭa-
śyante sūtrakāreṇa teṣāmapi pramaṅgaḥ syāditi, vidhigrahaṇa-
ntāvatsaprātaḥ savane savanamukhoyeṣvāhateṣūpahavamicchate lokadā-
royopākaraṇādi sidhyarthaṃ | avyapadeśa ityetadapi na vaktavyamityatra
brūmaḥ, śravyapadeśagrahaṇaṃ vikalpa sabhuccaya pratyāmnāyaprasaṅgapratiśedhārthaṃ,
eteṣāmasminneva śāstre darśanāt | vikalpastāvat hṛśyate,
abhiprayāyama bhiṣuṇvantyabhikrāntai samānantrābhiṣuvanti pratiṣṭhitya
iti savikalpa: syāditi | tathā rathantare vāgoṅkārayoḥ samucca-
yadarśanāt samuccayastu nānārthatvāditi | tathā pratyāmnāyopi
dṛśyate, sutyāyāṃ yajñamārathyaharahaḥ satre satraspaddhati | tadeteṣāṃ
prasaṅgomābhūdityata āha avyapadeśe iti | yaducyate sarvagrahaṇaṃ na
karttavyamityatra brūmaḥ, yadi hyayaṃ sarvasabdaṃ na kuryāttathāpi
mati ye tāṇḍake paripaṭhitā jyotiṣṭomādayaḥ sahasrasambatsarāntā-
steṣāmevādhikāro gamyeta | soyamācāryaḥ sarvaśabdaṃ karoti |

<<0020>> [1.1.2]
śrautasūtre |
-
yepi śākhāntare dṛṣṭāḥ ekāhāhīnamatreṣu bhū: sarvamedhacaturthasāra-
svatyādayasteṣāmevādhikāraḥ syāditi | yaducyate avikāragrahaṇa
na karttavyamityatra brūmaḥ, adhikāragrahaṇaṃ niyamārthaṃ | kathaṃ.
śrayamadhikāra prātideśikān sarvān adhikārān bādhitvā
tramamāpteḥ syāditi | tasmādyadutamārabdhavyaṃ sūtramiti tadyuktaṃ || 1 ||
evaṃ siddhe sarvādhikāre vakṣyatyācāryaḥ, mahanmevāca iti
kariṣyan pratiprantrayeteti, tatrāyaṃ maṃśayaḥ kimiyataiva pratimantraṇaṃ
kriyatāṃ śratha kṛsnena mantreṇeti | etasmin maṃśaye satyāhācāryaḥ,
mantra vidhiśvādigrahaṇena || 2 ||
tatra mantraśabdaḥ pratītaśabdārthaḥ kartṛpadārthako mahanmevācādiṣu
yajaḥṣu varttate | vidhīyate vidhānaṃ veti vidhiḥ | ādigrahaṇena
ādīyate’rtho’neneti trādi: | tryaṃ satrārthaḥ ādiggṛhītomantraḥ
kṛtsaḥ prayoktavya iti | anrocyate, yadyevamarthaḥ, satrārambho
na karttavyastarhi, ṛtepi etasmādavagamyeta etat, ādigrahīto

uktaṃ prahiṇuyāt prastoṭasubrahmaṇyo purastāt karmabhya iti tatra
subrahmaṇīya muktam anantaraṃ prastotrīyaṃ vaktavyam | tatra kramabhedasya
prayojanamuktam subrahmaṇyaprakaraṇeva sāmprataṃ prastotakarma vivakṣuridaṃ
sūtramārabhate, sarvatrānādeśa dūti | tatra padāni sarvatra anādeśe pari-
sāmāni prastotā gāyet svādhyāyavat skhāsu | tatra sarvaśabdo
niravaśeṣavācī | sarvavidhiviṣayo nirdeśaḥ sarvakratusvityarthaḥ | anādeśa
iti śrādeśādanyatra, ādeśaḥ yathā śrayaṃ sahohā dūti trirudgātā gāye-
diti | parisāmānīti karmanirdeśaḥ, paricchinnakarṭakāṇi sāmāni
parisāmāni parigataliṅgāni vā sāmāni parisāmānyucyante | prasto
teti kartṛnirdeśaḥ | gāyediti kriyā niddiśyate | svādhyāyavaditi
dharmucyate svādhyāyena tulyā kriyā svādhyāyavat khāsu, khākhi-
tyāśrayaviśeṣo niyamyate | svāskhaskhāmu ca sānnāṃ dayī vṛttirdṛśyate
sarvapadānāmarthaḥ | śratha samudāyārthaḥ | yānyetāni tārkṣyamāmādīni
udaṃgoyāntāni dovaṇīyādiṣūdavamānoyānteṣu karmasṛpadiśyante
etāni sarvāṇi prastoṭakarmeti | atrocyate, sarvatra grahaṇaṃ tāvatra karttavyam,
kimartham, śrakriyamāṇe’pi sarvatragrahaṇe pratyeṣyatetat yathā sarvatreti
* brāhmāyaṇoṭa pyevam |

<<0058>> śrotasūtre |
[1.5.1]
kayam vidhyavyapadeśe sarvakratvadhikāra iti vacanāt adhikāranivṛttyartha-
miti cet, dīkṣānupūrveṇa dīkṣitānāmiti tanna | kasmāt, prakaraṇa-
samāpta: | na prakṛtamatideśā bādhantiti nyāyopadeśāt | anādeśa
ityetadapi śakyamavaktum | kasmāta, sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ pravṛtti-
viṃdhīnām |
sāmānyo vidhirautsargikaḥ tasyāpavādo
viśeṣaḥ, tatra caitsargiko vidhirapavādena vādhiyyate, tasmācchakāma-
vakumanādeśadūti parisāmānoti ca vaktavyam kasmāta, sarvathā
saṃvyavahārārthīḥ saṃjñāḥ śākhe bhavanti | na cānayā saṃjñayā śākhe
maṃvyavahāro’sti | prastoṭagrahaṇamapyatiricyateva kasmāt prakṛtatvāt
prahiṇuyāt prastosubrahmaṇo iti, tena saṃyogādugādaprasaṅga iti cet,
tanna kasmāt asabhavāt svayaṃ vrajet kraya cai|pavasathyeveti | pratihattī
syāditi cet, tadapi na prakṛtahāniḥ syāt aprakṛtapratyayaśca |
prakṛto hi prastotā, aprakṛto hi pratihattī | atha gāyedityetadapi
atiricyateva sāma codyamānaṃ gānādanyatra kiṃ bhajate | svādhyāya-
vadityetadapi na vaktavyam | agṭahyamāṇaviśeṣaṃ sāma svādhyāyavadeva
bhavati, viśeṣastu yathā mandramivāya ādadītātha tārataramatha
tāratamamiti aniruka geyaṃ balbalānukuvatā geyam | akṣare-
ṇākṣareṇa pratiṣṭhāpayatodneyamiti | khāsvityetadapi na vattavyam
kasmāt, anyābhirasaṃyogāt | traviśeṣeṇādiśyamānaṃ khāmu ujjhilā
kathamakhāsu kriyate anyābhiramaṃyogaḥ tyattikasaṃyogāt
viśvedevā iti vasiṣṭhanihavamūhet, tathā svayonīni sarvatrābhi
rūpatarāṣyasvayonīni na iti | evaṃ sarveṣāṃ pratipadamuddhāra utaḥ |

<<0059>> lāyāyanī ye
[1.5.2]
athavocyate, prayojanamucyatām atrāha yaducyate, nārabdhavyānī-
tyārabdhavyānīti dhūmaḥ | kasmādārambhe vidhiprasiddheḥ | yattāvadu-
cate, sarvatra śabdo’tiricatiti tanna, na kevalamasmiṃśchākhe
śrayamādeśaḥ, anyatrāpi yathā adhvaryyavityāhodgāteti | yat
sarvatreti na brūyādviśvarūpāṇāṃ gānaṃ prastotuḥ syāt pariṇāmaśabda-
lāt ta āi sarvatrānādeśa dūti | ādeśagrahaṇamuktārthaṃ prathama-
sūtreva vikalpasamuccaya pratyāmnāyaprasaṅgo mābhūditi | yaducate
parimāmānīti na vaktavyam śāstre saṃvyavahārābhāvādityatra brūmaḥ |
asti saṃjñāmaṃvyavahāraḥ śākheṇa ca sampadatireko yathānyaiḥ parisāmabhi-
riti yaducyate | prakṛtatvāt prastotagrahaṇaṃ na karttavyamityatra brūmaḥ |
karttavyameva kasmānniyamārtham | vyāitisāmānugāpanañca prastotuḥ syā-
diti vyāitisāmāni gāpayed yajamānamityekaśrutividhānāt
udgātumabhūditi | atha yaduktaṃ gāyediti na vaktavyam sāma codya-
mānaṃ gāmakriyāṃ bhajatadūtyatra brūmaḥ | śrākhyātapracodanānnāsti doṣaḥ |
dṛśyante hi vākyānyubhayorvedalokayoḥ uccamānārthāni gamyamānārthīni
arthagṭahotāni ca | uccamānārthānāṃ tāvad yathādvāraṃ dīyatāmiti
yathā gamyamānārthadvāramiti doyatām apidhīyatāṃ beti, yathā
śīghramiti saṃgrahakāreṇa tathā vede jyotiṣṭomenātirātreṇa rddhi-
kāmo yajeteti | athaiṣa gauratheṣa āyuriti idamākhyātaprayoge na
doṣaḥ | atha yaduktaṃ gāyatrarathantaravadviśeṣagrahaṇabhāvāt kathamanya
dharmaṃ bhajatiti tasmāt svādhyāyavaditi na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ |
parisānāṃ prayoge saṃśaya: kimanudūhitānyananumaṃhatastobhāni

śrautasūtre |
kriyantām athoduhitānyevopasaṃhṛtastobhāni ca kriyantām kena
vā svareṇa kriyantāmiti eṣa saṃśaya: | ānāye kānicidanu-
saṃdatastobhāni padyante kānicidādyantasudhāni keṣucit pāda
śiṣṭā gītiḥ padyate | tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ, kiṃ tenaiva dharmeṇa yujyatā-
mathānyo dharma iti | tathodūhaḥ kiṃ prāpnoti caturthodāttatamāt
svarādvyantarānudūhati prāgupāyānna cet samānapuruṣavacane tṛtīyaprabhṛtī-
nāmudāttatamaḥ kaścit svaro bhavati, tamudūha ityācakṣate | tathāca
yajñe kriyatiti ca śāṅgīdīnāmudūhaḥ prāpnoti etasmin prāpte
svādhyāyavadityāha | ataḥ śāṅgīdiṣu udūho nivarttate anupadañca
stobhānusaṃhāraḥ syādityeṣa svādhyāyadharmaḥ | nanu yadyeṣa svādhyāyadharmaḥ,
kimarthamuddhṛtastobhāni padyante | uccate, lāghavārthamatrāha, yadi
lāghavārthamuddhāraḥ, kimarthamanyānyanupadasundhānīti ucyate stobha-
sthānasvara nidarśanārtham | kathaṃ punaretadgamyate yathā nidarśanārtham na
niyamārthamiti nidarśanārthameveti gamyatām smṛtileśāt, smṛti-
nīma amūla āgama: pāramparyyamityarthaḥ | evaṃ viśiṣṭāḥ saranti |
padāya padāya stobhā anuvarttantiti liṅgam, yadihakāreṇā-
bhyastamiti ca, kathaṃ punaretadgamyate, yathā nidarśanārthamidamiti |
padāya padāya stobhā anuvarttantiti rātoghna evāyaṃ vidhiriti,
neti brūmahe | nityānuvādo’yantasthāhāvohāva iti slobhāṃstobhati
viśvaṃ samantriṇaṃ daha viśvaṃ samantriṇaṃ daheti | tadā aticchandaḥ su
bhavati ya saptapadāsu bhavati tasya trirnidhanamiti avagamyate
nityānuvāda iti | pāñcavidhyopapattesānumaṃhāraḥ karttavya iti |

<<0081>> [1.6.50 ]
sarveṣāṃ kriyā veti ekeṣāmadhvaryūṇāṃ prathamayajena pravṛñjyādityāra-
bhyate, tatra śārṅgādīnāmasambhavāt tārkṣyamāmādīnāmapyakriyā prāpnoti,

metadarthaṃ sūtramārabhyate, kiñca sarvakarmāṇi upakramya samāpayedākrato-
rapavargāt, yathā śāstre’sminnācāryyāṃ vipratipattayo dṛśyante tasyāṃ
te yaḥ sutyā gautamasya nārmedhāntitye ke’dyaḥ sutyā śāṇḍilyasyānāhānaṃ
dhānañjaya iti evamādiṣu yenaivācāryyamatenopakrameta tenaiva samāpayet
vidhisaṃrambhānna kuryyāt tathā udgātāro brahmā subrahmaṇyāsa upakramya
khāni karmāṇi samāpayeran anyonyasya karma na kuryyāt tathā kāmye
karmaṇi prārabdhe arddhasamāpteva yadi na phalāvāptiḥ sthāna ca tatphala-
mevāsau kāmāvāptiriti kṛtvā viramet lokavata nidānam iha hi
avaśiyyata evārthaḥ tadarthaṃ samāpayet kaḥ punarasāvarthaḥ nityaṃ
svīśaḥ bravīti tathāpyāḍaruddhārtheva khanvayambhavati anukhanvarthaḥ
śrutyarthī anvavayantīti nidānaṃ svarge nitye dṛṣṭaṃ prāyaścittiriti
tathā yajamānanimittāyāmāpadi prāptāyāṃ na tatkālameva vira-
met ekeṣāṃ vidhiḥ dotitaścedantarākāryo mriyeta maraṇanta karmeti
tattathā sati samāpayedeva uktaṃ hi ato’nya āhārāta gataprāṇava-

vā bhagnaṃ vānusamāva hedevaṃ vā ahaṃ yajñasthāto’dhikariṣyāmoti

brūyādatha vedimākrāmethurmṛdā śithireti sarveṣāmugāṭaṇaṃ yugapat-
karmocyate, tasya ko vidhiriti taṃ vivakṣurāha, yugapatkarmasthiti
yugapaditi yānyekavelāyāmeteṣu yugapatkarmasu sahakarṭakeṣu karmasu
sarveṣu sarvaśabdaḥ niravaśeṣavācī udgāturdakṣiṇa bāhu anu prastotā
* drāhmāyaṇoṭapyevam |

[1.8.3]

na kuryyādedyākramaṇādiṣu karmasu tadidhānaṃ pratīyate so’yamācāryyaḥ

prāyaṇīyo’tirātreovedatrirātraścai keṣā madhvaryūṇāmasamāpta evāini prāta-

<<0102>> [1.6.18]
śrautasūtre |
bahiṣpavamāne yāsu yāsu stotraṃ kariṣyantaḥ syuḥ atha purastāceti
kasmāducyate upariṣṭāñceti vaktavye sarvathā upariṣṭācchabdaḥ purastāt
kriyāmapekṣate samvandhiśabdādatrocca te stotrasambandhātpurastājapopari-
ṭājjapayo: sāmakalpita chandovikāraḥ prāpnoti ato’yamācāryyaḥ
purastāceti bravīti tena kiṃ naivarcaḥ sāmikaṃ dharmamapekṣante ya evau-
tpattikaḥ svādhyāyadharmalenaiva prayujyeranniti kathaṃ punaretadamukta
gamyate yatharcaḥ sāmikaṃ chandovikāraṃ gṛhantīti uccate śruteḥ
śrutirhi na kiṣṭaṃ karmaṇa naśaditi bṛhatyaḥ satyobhyārambheṇa jagatyaḥ
eṣo’sya dhārayā suta dūti kakubhaḥ satyobhyārambheṇa triṣṭubha iti ca atra
na kiṣṭaṃ karmaṇa naśadityekaiva bṛhatī tathā eṣo’sya dhārayāsuta itye-
kaiva kakup tatra satyā jagatyo vikāre bṛhatyaḥ kakubhaḥ satya iti
bahuvacanasyāsambhavaḥ tadevaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtrakāro yatnamārabhate, kathaṃ
purastājapopariṣṭājjapayoravikāraḥ syāditi atreocyate yadyevaṃ bṛhatyaḥ
satyaḥ kakubhaḥ satya iti asya bahuvacanasya kathamarthavattvamiti uccate,
pragāthadharmaṃ gṛholā bravīti brāhmaṇaṃ eṣa pragāthānāṃ dharmaḥ prathamañchandaḥ-
kriyā tathā pragātheṣu prathamañchandaḥ kriyā taccoditatvāditi evametaṃ
sāmānyaṃ pragāthadharmaṃ gṛhīlā brāhmaṇamāha, bṛhatya: satya ityādi eva-
metad brāhmaṇamarthavadbhavatīti śratha purastādupariṣṭācceti vaktavye purastā-
cchabde caśabdaḥ kimarthaṃ kriyate, ucyate niyamārthaṃ yadyapi pramādāt
kayañcit purastājjapo na kriyeta upariṭājjapaḥ kriyetaiva na sanniyoga-
śiṣṭāvetāviti kṛtvā upariṣṭājjapo nivarttate, sanniyoga śiṣṭānāmanya-
tamāpāye ubhayorapyapāya iti || 18 ||

[2.7.3]
śratha saptamī kaṇḍikā |
atha dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭheran samastenottarayoḥ savanayoriti
gautama śāṇḍilyāyanau || 1 ||
uktaṃ savanasaṃsthāsu praśāstroktā yathetamaparayā dvārā niṣkramya paścime-
nāgnīprīyaṃ vahirvedi mūtraṃ kuryuriti tadyadi tāvanikramaṇānantaraṃ
mūtroccāre kurvanti tataḥ kṛtaśocā trācāntodakāḥ yadidamādecyate
tat kuryuḥ atha mūtroccāre naiva kuryuḥ tadā yathokrena vidhinā niṣkramyā
thānantaraṃ dhiṣṇyānupatiṣṭheran samastena uktaṃ tatraiva tiṣṭhantaḥ sarvānsa
manvokṣamāṇaḥ pātameti etat samastopasthānam anenottarayoḥ
savanayorupatiṣṭheran evaṃ gautama śāṇḍilyāyanāvācāryāvāhatuḥ || 1 ||

<<0200>> śrautasūtre |
[2.11.3]
tṛtīyasavane sarveṣu stotreṣu samāpteṣu bhakṣayitvā camasaṃ stoma-
vimocanaṃ kuryuḥ ṛtasya tvetyanena yajuṣā, natu tat kimidaṃ tṛtīyasavana-
grahaṇaṃ yadā sarveṣu stotreṣu samāptevvityuktam ucyate idantāvadyajurupari
sandhibhakṣātmamānnātaṃ tatra vimocanaṃ yajuṣā tasminneva krame prāpnoti
ataḥ tṛtīyasavanagrahaṇaṃ tāvatkrayate kathaṃ na kevalamupari sandhibhakṣāt
stoma vimocanaṃ syāt yasyāṃ yasyāṃ saṃsthāyāṃ kratuḥ samāpyate tasyā-
ntasyāṃ saṃsthāyāṃ syāditi atha sarvagrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti cet sto
sviti bahuvacanasāmarthyātmiddhe sarvatve idamucyate idaṃ stomavimo-
canaṃ kratvantastotre dṛṣṭaṃ pratistotrañca stomayojanaṃ bhavati yuktasya ca
vimocanaṃ bhavatyeva tasya ca yuktasya stomasya yasmin kāle vimo-
canamityeṣa maṃśayaḥ ataḥ sarvagrahaṇaṃ karotyācāryaḥ kathaṃ pūrveṣvapi
stotreṣu ekaikasmin stotre bhakṣayitvā stomaṃ vimuñceyuḥ atra tu tṛtīya-
savane kathamiti || 1 ||
dakṣiṇaiḥ pāṇibhiḥ kuśāḥ saṃlobhayeyuḥ || 2 ||
saṃlobhanaṃ ekatrīkaraṇaṃ kuryuḥ || 2 ||
185
yajamānavācanādanantaramatra vā yajamānaṃ vācayettantave-
mā jyotiṣetyasāvanumātanu hi jyotiṣeti yathājyeṣṭha
putrāṇāṃ nāmāni gṛhṇīyāt || 3 ||
* drahmāyaṇoṭapyevam |
drāhmāyaṇenaitena sūtracatuṣṭayaṃ kṛtam |

<<0201>> lāyāyanī ye
[2.11.5]

vācanaṃ etasmādanantaraṃ etat karma kuryāt tadacyate atra vā asmin
kāle kuśānāṃ saṃlobhanaṃ kṛtvā kuryuḥ iti vikalpaḥ tantave mā jyo-
tiṣetyuktvā asāvanumātanuhi jyotiṣeti yathā jyeṣṭha putrāṇaṃ
nāmāni gṛhīyāt asāviti sarvanāmasthāne nāma gṛhīyāt yo yo
jyaṣṭo yathā jyeṣṭhaṃ prayogastu tantave mā jyotiṣā yajñadatta anu-
mātanuhi viṣṇumitra anumātanuhi somabhūte anumātanuhi jyotiṣā

<<0212>> [2.12.18]
śrautasūtre |
sarvakratuṣu jānīyāt, nanu uktaḥ sarvakratvadhikāra iti tat kimidaṃ puna-
rucyate sarvakratuṣu vidyāditi uccate antaprajñāpanārthaṃ kathaṃ atha
vidhyavyapadeśe sarvakratvadhikāra iti etadādividherayamanta iti evaṃ
sarvakratuṣu vidyāditi apara āha, sarvakratoradhikāraḥ sarvakratvadhikāra
iti sarvakratuḥ jyotiṣṭomaḥ kutaḥ śruteḥ eṣa vā prathamo yajñānāmi
tyukāha yathā vā idamagnerjātādamayo vijñayanta evametasmādadhyanye
yajñā vihviyanta ityuktvāi yo hi tridṛdanyaṃ yajñakratumāpadyate sa tandī-
payatotyetadāyukkāi etadyadāhureko yajña ityetaddhi sarve jyotiṣṭomā
bhavantīti etadvidhānamāpadyamānāḥ sarve jyotiṣṭomā bhavantīti
sarvakratuṣu jyotiṣṭomaḥ tadādāveva sarvakratvadhikāra iti jyotiṣṭomā-
dhikāraḥ teṣāṃ punaruktadoṣo nāsti evaṃ jyotiṭomavidhiṃ sarvakratuṣu
vidyāt adhikavidheśca pratyāhāraṃ kuryāt || 18 ||
iti dvitīyasya dvādaśī kaṇḍikā |
iti dvitīyaḥ prapāṭhakaḥ samāptaḥ |

<<0213>> tṛtīyaḥ prapāṭhakaḥ |
atha prathamā kaṇḍikā |
ṣoड़śisāmnā stoṣyamāṇo yathāsanamupavigya iviḍīnaṃ
gatvā ṣoḍa़ śigrahamave kṣetodgātā yasmādanya iti || 1 ||
uktaṃ sārvakratukaṃ sāmānyavidhānaṃ sāmprataṃ ṣoड़śino guṇavidhāna-
mucyate sārvakratuko’yaṃ ṣoड़śī daśarātrike caturtho’hanyutpannaḥ atraiva
cāsya hiraṇyaṃ sampradānaṃ ṣoड़śinā stuvatityevamādayo dharmāḥ paṭhitāḥ
teṣāṃ vidhānaṃ vivaturāha ṣoड़śisāmrā stoyyamāṇa iti, nanu ukta
tvayā caturthe’hani ṣoड़śī utyanna iti tat prakaraṇe caiva dharmā vaktavyāḥ
syuḥ tat kimidaṃ viprakaraṇe guṇavidhānam ārabhyata iti yadā ca
tasminneva prakaraṇe yasmādanyo na paro asti jāta ityetadādi mantra
vidhāyoktam udgātā grahamavekṣeta iti dañcāveca vidhānaṃ kimartha-
miti cet atrocyate tadidam avekṣaṇaṃ prakaraṇe stotrānte uktaṃ tatrāyaṃ
saṃśayaḥ kiṃ kālaṃ prati tāvat kiṃ tasminneva kāle’vekṣaṇamathānyasmi
niti tathā kiṃ havirddhānasthasyeva athāvekṣaṇapravṛttiḥ sadasoti avekṣaṇaṃ
hi sadasi pravṛtta momānāṃ saumyasya ca tathā ete dharmā hiraṇyasampra-
dānādayaḥ caturthotpādāḥ ayañca ṣoड़śo prakaraṇāntareṣvapi śrūyate
māhyāyaṇoṭa pyevam |

<<0214>> śrautasūtre |
sarvastomātirātrādiṣu tat kimete dharmāḥ prakaraṇasyasya bhavanti uta

aprākṛtastu na vacanādikkatīrbhajata iti ato’yamācārya etā-
nmohān parititīrṣuḥ sārvakratukānantaraṃ ghoड़śino vidhānamārabhate
katham etaṃ sārvakratukaṃ vidhānaṃ ṣoड़śinaḥ syāditi yadi hyetaṃ vidhāna-
mācāryaḥ prakaraṇa āmnāyasya tadviṣayamevābhaviṣyat tanmābhūdatā vipra-
karaṇa ārammaḥ ṣoḍa़śisānā stoṣyamāṇaḥ yathāsanamupaviśya havirddhānaṃ
gatvā ṣoड़śigrahamaveceta udgātā yasmādanya iti eṣa padānāṃ vicchedaḥ
artho vakṣyate ghoड़śimāmneti karttṛkaraṇalakṣaṇā ḍhatīyā stoṣyamāṇa
dūti bhaviṣyatkālopadeśaḥ yathāsanamupaviśya saṃsthāyāsane niḥsṛpya
samastopasthānaṃ kṛtvā kṛtlena vā akṛtvā vā svasminnāsana upaviśya
havirddhānaṃ gatvā ṣoड़śigrahamavekṣeta udgātā yasmādanya ityanena mantreṇa,
nanu ṣoड़śisāmneti sāmagrahaṇaṃ kimarthaṃ yadāyaṃ ṣoड़śiśabdaḥ kṛte’pi
sāmagrahaṇāt stotravācī bhaviṣyatyeva ayaṃ hi ṣoड़śiśabdaḥ triṣu
varttate stotre grahe saṃsthāyāmiti stotre tāvat yogāya trīṣu dipadāṣu

tṛtīyamavane prajanayatīti svatrāyatane ṣoड़śī gṛhyatiti ca saṃsthāyāṃ
so’bravīt ṣoड़śī te’yaṃ yajñakratura sviti so’yaṃ ṣoड़śiśabdaḥ prayu-

evaṃ maśakaḥ paṭhati trābhilavike ṣaṣṭhe’hani indrāyendo marutvata
iti gāyatrañcāśvatañca sakṛdiṣovṛdhīyaṃ kuryyāt mṛjyamānaḥ
suhatyetyaiḍañcautorandhaṃ trinidhanañcāyyāsya sakṛt samantaṃ kuryyāt sakṛt
saladityukrena vai spaṣṭaṃ ṃ katarasminnabhiplava iti so’yamācāryyaḥ spaṣṭī-
drāhmāyaṇoṭa pyevam |

anyatrāpi yadā kāleyaṃ pavamāne syāt tatrā’pyetasya stotrīyaṃ śaṃsaye-
dacchāvākena yathā viśvajitīti || 18 ||
sarvatrendrakratuṃ brāhmaṇācha sināīṃ viṣuvataḥ prāgati-
rātrāt || 18 ||
ūrddha viṣuvataḥ yānyahāni teṣu sarvescindrakratu brāhmaṇācchaṃsi
naḥ śaṃsayet prāgatirātrāt udayanīyam atirācaṃ varjayitvā sarvaśabdo
niravaśeṣavācī || 18 ||

śratha saptamī kaṇḍikā |
245
daśamasya; bahiṣpavamānaṃ dvitīyaprabhṛtīnāṃ pañcānāmahā-
manurūpāḥ prathamācca bahiṣyavamānaṃ tannavarcam || 1 ||
*
daśānāṃ pūraṇaḥ daśamaḥ daśamasyeti sambandhalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭho bahi-
vyavamānamiti stotropadeśaḥ dvitīyaprabhṛmīnāmiti nidadhyarupadeśaḥ
prabhṛtiśabdaḥ ādyābhidhāyī pañcānāmiti saṃkhyā hāmiti aha-
nirdeśa: anurūpā iti bahiṣpavamānaṃ tannavacaṃ navarcamiti maṃjñā
bahiṣpavamānasya ādyadvitīyāntyāstṛcaḥ pratipadanurūpaparyāmaḥ prathamā-
ccāhnaḥ bahiṣpavamānantannavacaṃ navarcamiti saṃjñā etaddaśamasyāho bahi-
ṣpavamānam atrocyate yadā tāvadeva bahiṣpatramānaṃ dāśamikaṃ klṛpta-
meva sarvaṃ brāhmaṇe pañcānāmanāmanurūpaiḥ pratyavayanti navarce bhavanti
yā evāmū: prayacchan yā śrāvadadhātīti ca sambandho’sya darśitaḥ
prāthamikasya navarcastha vāruṇyekā bhavati ādityekā bhavatīti ca
liṅgacodanā tat kimidaṃ siddhe sati punarārabhyate daśamasya bahiṣpava-
mānamiti ucyate, trācāryyasyeyaṃ pravṛttiḥ yatra hi kālo vā
viśeṣo vā kañcidvivakṣito bhavati tatra siddhasyāpi sato vidhiḥ puna-
rupādānaṃ karoti yathā ekatrike madyaḥ sarvaṃ kuryurekadīkṣastyupasatka
iti gautamastasya gāyatrapārśvamārbhavo yā ruceti purojityamiti
śāṇḍilya iti etad vivatuḥ siddhamidaṃ gāyatrapārśva punarāmanati
* drāhmāyaṇo’pyebam |

<<0261>> 246
jādyāyanī ye
[3.7.1]
evamiha vidhiśeṣa vivakṣuḥ siddhopādānaṃ karoti kaḥ punarvidhiḥ
śiṣyate yo vaktavyaḥ uccate, brāhmaṇaṃ pañcānāmahāmanurūpaiḥ pratyavaya-
nīti tathā vaktavyam etadarthaṃ siddhamapi santaṃ punarādadate ucyate
yadyevaṃ siddhe’pi sati punarādadate daśamagrahaṇaṃ tāvanna karttavyaṃ kasmāt
nāvamikaṃ vidhānamukta śeṣo’pi vidhirucyamānaḥ saṃkhyānāt daśa-
mādanyatra ca bhavet tasmāddaśamagrahaṇaṃ śakyamavatu bahiṣpavamānagrahaṇaṃ
śakyameva vaktu bahiṣpavamānasya grahaṇasya kiṃ kāraṇaṃ tacchakyatvāt tat
vivaktavyam atra heāturājyādārabhya susamiddho na śrāva hetyetasmāddāśa-
mikāni stotrāṇi pratyakṣaśiṣṭāni tasmāt kāraṇaṃ na vaktavyaṃ dvitīya-
prabhṛtīnāmityetadapyanārabdhavyameva yasmādvitīyaprabhṛtiṣvahaḥsu vahi-
ṣyavamānadvitīyāstṛcasteṣāmanurūpā iti saṃjñā pavaskhendovṛṣāsuta
ityetadādīnāṃ ahāmanurūpā ityetacca na vaktavyaṃ kasmāt ukta pañcā-
nāmahāmanurūpaiḥ pratyavayantīti prathamācca bahiṣpavamānantanavarca-
mityetadapi na vaktavyaṃ kasmāt uktaṃ navarce bhavatīti yā evāmū:
prayacchan yā śravadadhāti tā etā udasyatīti prāthamikenaiva
bahiṣpavamānena sambandhaṃ darśayati tasmāt sarvameva sūtraṃ nārabdhavyam
ārambha vā prayojanaṃ vaktavyam atreocyate, yaduktaṃ nārabhavyamityārabhavya-
miti brūmaḥ śeṣavidhyarthaṃ yattāvaducyate daśamagrahaṇaṃ na kartavyamiti
atra brūmaḥ karttavyameva chandomā iti paṭhati abhyasaṅgyaḥ pañcāsa-
tvāraḥ chandomā viśvajidatirātra iti tatredaṃ saṃkhyānato navamaṃ tatrāyaṃ
maṃśayaḥ kimatra dāśamikaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavatyata utpattikatvāt
nāvamikaṃ mābhūditi yāvatā nidānakāreṇāpi vicāritaṃ kathaṃ

<<0262>> [3.7.2]
śrautasūtre |
daśamadharmā mānasamiti karttavyā ityeke taccāharjāyata iti aka-
rtavya ityaparamadaśamañca luptaśca daśarātra iti so’yamācārtho’niya
mārthaṃ daśamagrahaṇaṃ karoti kathaṃ adaśame’pyetasmin bahiṣpavamānaṃ
syāditi, atha yaduktaṃ bahiṣpavamānagrahaṇaṃ na karttavyamityatra brūmaḥ
bahiṣpavamānagrahaṇaṃ kriyate niyamārthaṃ kathaṃ etasminnahani na kadā-
cidanyaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ syāditi kutaḥ punarāśaṅkā yathānya bahi-
vyavamānaṃ syāditi ucyate, maśakaḥ paṭhati dvādaśāhavicāreṣu api
vā pratipadāvevānyonyasyāḥ sthānaṃ vyatiharediti na kadācidapi
bahiṣpavamānasya vikāraḥ syāt daśame’hanīti, atha yadukta dvitīya-
prabhṛtonāmiti na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ anyonyasya sthānaṃ dvitīya-
prabhṛtīnāmeva syuḥ, śratha yadukta pañcānāmityatra brūmaḥ śravidyamāne-
vvapi pañcānāmeva kuryuḥ yathā chando bhavati daśarātre, śratha yadukta-
mahāmiti na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ aharvyatyāso’pyānupūrvyeṇa syāt,
atha yaduktamanurūpā iti na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ anurūpagrahaṇaṃ
sāptamikapratiṣedhārthaṃ kathaṃ samūhite dvādaśāhe etā anurūpā na syu-
riti yeṣāmevānurūpā saṃjñā tā eveti, atha yaduktaṃ prathamācca bahi-
ṣpavamānaṃ tannavarcamityetadapi na vaktavyamityatra brūmaḥ avachinnabahi-
ṣpavamānaṃ klṛptaṃ chandomā mati daśarātre tanmābhūditi tasmāt sūtra-

yābhyo hiṅkāraṃ pṛthak nānetyarthaḥ stotrīyābhyo hiṃkāraṃ kuryu: trike
stomena ukta parācībhiḥ stuvantīti evaṃ parākkam trastomayogā yaja-

pratihārabelāyāṃ pratichattīpānyāt || 2 ||
252
lāthāyanoya

uttama prastutyaiṣeti hotāramokṣeta* || 3 ||

*

kṣaṇena vijñāpayantaḥ brahmaṃstoṣyāmaḥ praśāstarityataḥ ārabhya samīkṣaṇa-

śrautasūtre |
daha mahāvrataprakaraṇe trayodaśaparimādaḥ paṭhitā brāhmaṇena purastā-
dāhavanīyamupatiṣṭhanta ityata ārabhya yāvadgārhapatyopasthānamiti tad-
nantaraṃ paṭhati āmandīmāruhyādgāyatīti parimādagānānantaraṃ mahā-
vratasya stavanaṃ darśayati teṣāṃ parimādāṃ kriyāvidhiṃ vivakṣuridaṃ sūtra-
mārabhate mahāvratasya pṛṣṭhe upākṛte yukvā stomaṃ parimādo gāyediti
mahāvrata iti karmaṇo nāmadheyaṃ tasyeti sambandhalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī pṛṣṭhamiti
stotrasaṃjñā tasmin pṛṣṭhe upākṛte upākaraṇaṃ nāmādhvaryavaṃ karma upā-
varttadhvamiti yukvā stomaṃ stomayojanaṃ kṛtvā yathoktena mantreṇa pari-
māda iti saṃjñā parimādbhiñcaranti tvak ca vā etalloma ca mahāvratasya
yatparimāda iti gāyediti kriyopadeśaḥ bhāṇḍitāyana ityācārya-
matasaṃkīrttanaṃ eṣa sūtrārtha: mahāvratasya krato: hoṭapṛṣṭhe upākṛte
lomayojanaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ parimādagānamiti ucyate, daśamamahaḥ nirava
śeṣa mukkaṃ tasmādanantaraṃ mahāvratamānā taṃ dvādaśāhasya dvādaśāhāni
mahāvratañceti tadevamānantaryādeva prāpte mahāvratake vidhā parimāda-
samvandhāca yāvatā mahāvratādanyatra parimādo na bhavanti tat kimidaṃ
mahāvratagrahaṇaṃ mahāvratasya pṛṣṭhe iti uccate niyamārtha mahāvratagrahaṇaṃ

dvividhamabhiplavameke ācāyā: kalpayanti diḥ prakāraṃ dvividhaṃ
kiṃ dvividhaṃ upavatī agrīyavatī ca vyatyāsampatipadī vyatyasya vyatyasya
rathantaravāītāni cājyāni vyatyāsameveti prakṛtam rāthantareṣu

doni rāthantarāṇyājyāni bāīteṣu pavastra vāco agriya iti pratipat
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha ityetadādīni bāītānyājyāni etadvai vidhyam ||18||
ājyapratipadāvāśanakāve antya pārthayāme vā bārhatānāṃ

evaṃ vā dvaividhya syāt śrājyapratipadī śrājyañca pratipañcājya-

mādhyandinārbhavayorauiśanakāve anya svayonyabhīvarttaḥ eṣa prathamatṛtīya-

agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha iti heāturājyaṃ mādhyandinārbhavayoḥ pavamānayoḥ
pārthayāme antye śvetatu abhīvarttaḥ eṣa dvitīyacaturthaṣaṣṭheṣu dravya

ini seomubvāṇaḥ sloṭabhiriti ānūparathantare tvacayoḥ hārāyaṇa-

pavanta indava dūti gaurīvitabṛhatotṭacayoḥ trākūpāramadhu prannidhana-
krauñcāni sāmaṭaca: madhye nidhanamaiड़ krauñce caturthe purojito vo
andhasa iti nānadāndhīgavaṇyāvāśvāni sāmaṭacaḥ bṛhattṛce ete eva
vyūḍha़kalpaḥ samūhakalpe somāḥ pavanta indavaḥ iti gaurīvitamadhu-
nidhane ṭacayo: krauñce dve ākūpārañca sāmaṭacaḥ bṛhati samūḍhe
pṛṣṭhye || 8 ||
abhovarttakāleye vṛhatoyvanukarūpayediti gautamaḥ || 8 ||

[4.6.13]

kāyā3 agniṣṭomā3 ityevamukkāha tadāirvivavadhamiva vā eta-

jyotiṣāmayanavikalpā || 1 ||
dūha gavāmayanasya ṣaṣṭhyadhikaṃ triṃśataṃ paṭhitānyahāni brāhmaṇena
saṃvatsaravikalpācāneke śrūyante jyotirnacatrādayasteṣāṃ kalpanā cikī-

uttare pakṣasyānyasya || 3 ||

<<0335>> lāyāyanīye
[4.8.7]
320
hobhiḥ ūno bhavati nākṣatraḥ nakṣatramammitaḥ saptaviṃśino māsā bhavanti
tatra saptaviṃśatirnakṣatrāṇīti || 4 ||
ṣaṣṭhādyasyābhiśavasya sthāne jyotigāśca jyotirevāvṛtta
sa navono nākṣatra eva trayodaśī* || 5 ||
ṣaṣṭhasya māsasya ya ādyo’bhiśavaḥ tasya sthāne jyotirgauca syātāṃ
jyotirevāvṛttaḥ syāt na gauḥ uktaṃ tatra yadādito’ntatastaduī viṣu-
vata iti sa bhāvanāt saṃvatsarānnavabhirahobhirūnaḥ catvāryahāni pūrva-

trayodaśī tatrāpi saptaviṃśina eva māsāḥ trayodaśa bhavanti || 5 ||
yugmamāseṣvādyasyābhiśavasya sthāne tatpañcācaḥ sa ṣaḍū-
naścāndramasaḥ * || 6 ||
yugmamāseṣu dvitīyacaturthaṣaṣṭheṣu prathamasyābhiplavasya sthāne tatpa
ñcāhaḥ abhiplavapañcāhaḥ tatra yadādito’ntatastaduī viṣuvata ityetadanu-
varttate evaṃ sāvanāt saṃvatsarāt ṣaḍbhirahobhirūnacāndramasaḥ eṣā
cāndramasī gatiḥ || 6 ||

<<0341>> [4.8.1]
ukta gavāmayanaṃ savikalpaṃ sāmprataṃ brahmatva vivakṣitaṃ indro
havai viśvāmitrāyokthamuvāca vasiṣṭhāya brahmavāgukthamityeva viśvā-
mitrāya mano brahma vasiṣṭhāya tadā etadāsiṣṭhaṃ brahmāpi haivaṃvidaṃ
vā vāsiṣṭhaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ kurvīteti evaṃ brāhmaṇaparāmarśaḥ kriyate
udgātre tasya brahmaṇaḥ karmocyate tadvivacarāha sarvatra brahmā dakṣi
etaḥ udaṅmukhaḥ kuryyāditi sarvatra sarvakarmasvityarthaḥ sarvaśabdo nirava-
śeṣavācī brahmeti karttā niddiśyate dakṣiṇata iti dikparigrahaḥ
kriyate kasya dakṣiṇataḥ uccate, karmaṇaḥ kriyamāṇasya dakṣiṇe pradeśe
syāt uktaṃ tasmādbrāhmaṇaṃ dakṣiṇata āsayatīti udaṅmukha iti karma-
sadamukhatā nirdiśyate brāhmaṇa: kuyāditi kriyāpadeśaḥ sarveṣāṃ
karmaṇāṃ kriyamāṇānāṃ dakṣiṇatā brahmā syāditi eṣa sūtrārtha: home-
bhyoynyatkarma udaṅmukhaḥ kuryāt homastu prāṅmukha eva prāmukhakaraṇa-
cānādeśa iti atreocyate, sarvagrahaṇantāvanna karttavyaṃ kiṃ kāraṇam
adhikṛtatvāt sarvakarmaṇāṃ vidhyavyapadeśe sarvakratvadhikāra iti so’yaṃ
vidhiravyapadeśe ādiśyamānaḥ sārvakratuko bhaviṣyatyeva tasmāt sarvagrahaṇaṃ
śakyamavaktum, śratha punaḥ kriyate kāraṇaṃ vaktavyam uccate, atra tāva-
dayaṃ sarvaśabdo’dhikāranivṛttyarthaḥ satreṣu sarvānadhvaryurdīcayedityeṣo’dhi
kāraḥ pravṛttaḥ tasmāt sarvaśabdo yukto brahmaṇaḥ karmādau ucyate,
yadyevaṃ tathāpi na karttavyaḥ sarvaśabdaḥ kasmāt arthasamāpteḥ yo’sā sajā-
dhikāraḥ pravṛttaḥ tasyārthaḥ samāptaḥ kiñcānyat na prakṛtamatideśā
bādhantiti ca nyāyopadeśāt na hyātideśiko vidhi: sāmānyasyā-
dhikārasya pravṛttasya bādhako bhavati tasmāt sarvaśabdastadavasya eva
226
mādyāyanīye

<<0342>> śrautasūtra |
[B.E.R]
ucyate, evaṃ tāvadayaṃ sarvaśabdaḥ śeṣavidhyupasaṃgrahārtho’stu udgātra
somamadhikṛtyotpannaṃ sarvakratvadhikāra iti so’yamācāryyaḥ sarvaśabda
karoti kathaṃ etadbrahmatva' pākahaviḥ someṣu sarveṣu sthāditi ucyate,
yadyevamarthaṃ sarvagrahaṇaṃ tathāpi na karttavyameva prakriyamāṇe’pyetasmin na
gamyata evaitat yathā sarvatreti kathaṃ pākayajñādīn vacyati ekāmā
yajñāsteṣāṃ hovyatsa tūṣṇomupaviśet agnyādheye dakṣiṇyā dvārā prapadya
cātuṣpāśyannirvasyatsu, dvaṣṇīmupaviśet iddhyādiṣu sarveṣu yajuṣopa
viśet mithunau dakṣiṇāncārambhaṇīyāyāmiṭau amāvāsyāyāndoina-
pavitre mārjayerannāpohiṣṭhīyābhiḥ cāturmāsyeṣu varuṇapraghāsānāṃ-
stambayajurharivyatsu, yajuṣopaviśet paśūnāṃ yūpājatiṃ heāyyatsu, tūṣṇī-
mupaviśet mautrāmaṇyāṃ surākarmakhātrājamāsīteti evamekaviṃśati-
saṃsthāpi yajñe middhe brahmatve sarvagrahaṇaṃ na tadavasthameva tasmānna karttavya-
miti ucyate, karttavyameva trakriyamāṇe etasmin ye somāṅgabhṛtāḥ
pākahaviryajñāstāseṣu na pratīyeta yahārṣadratamadhikṛtya navoti naitandha-
vānāmāmaḥ sarasvatyānteṣāmeko’dhvaryustasmin vatsaramagnimindhīta taye
kāgneḥ paricayyā tayeti saṃvatsarādūīṃ pariṇamanasthālo kurukṣetre tasyā-
manonādhāya yathākālamanvārambhaṇīyayeṣṭā prasajyeteti tathā kaiṇḍa-
pāyino māmandīkṣitā bhavanti te māsi māsi somaṃ krīvanti teṣāṃ
dvādaśopasadamupasadbhiritvā somamupanahya māsamagnihotra juhati
māsandarśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajate māsa vaiśvadevena māsambaruṇapraghāmaiḥ
māmaṃ sākamedhairmāsaṃ unāśīti evamete pākahaviryajñāḥ somāṅga-
bhūtā dṛṣṭāḥ tadakriyamāṇe sarvaśabde eteṣvevetatva na pratīyeta

<<0343>> māthāyanī ye
[4.8.2]
tanmābhūdityata āha sarvatreti ucyate, yadyevamartha tathāpi na karttavyam
asminneva pākahaviryajñaprakaraṇajñāpakāni vacyante yathā phūlagave ca
balīn kriyamāṇānanugacchet iśyādiṣu sarveṣu yajuṣopaviśet etat
sarveṣṭīnāṃ brahmatvam aṅgabhūtānāṃ vetyetadukta bhavati paśūnāṃ yūpājati
hāvyatma yajuṣopaviśet vapāyāṃ hutāyāmidamāpa iti cātvāle
mārjayitvā sarvapaśūnāṃ yathārthaṃ syāt aṅgabhūtānāṃ cānaṅgabhṛtā-
nāñceti siddhe ekaviṃśatisaṃsthe yajñe brahmatve sarvatragrahaṇaṃ tadavasyameva
tasmācchasyamakarttum uccate, na karttavyaṃ karttavyameva stha tāva-
tsarvaśabdasya brahmaṇaiva samānādhikaraṇamastu sarvatra brahmā sava jāyata iti
sarvatraṃ sarvatra cāsau brahmā ca sarvatra brahmā kathaṃ sarvaṃ trāyate evaṃvidaṃ
6 vā eṣa brahmāṇamanugāvyetyevamadhikṛtyāha brāhme vaikartika-
kurutaścābhirakṣati evaṃvit ha vai brahmā yajña yajamānaṃ sarvaścarlijo-
’bhirakṣati tasmādevaṃvidameva brāhmaṇaṃ kurvīteti so’yaṃ sūtrakāraḥ
evaṃlakṣaṇaṃ brahmāṇaṃ darśayati sarvatra brahmeti kiñcānyat yatra ca brahmaṇaḥ
karmāsti sarveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ kriyamāṇānāṃ subrahmaṇyaprabhṛtīnāṃ brahmā hi
dakṣiṇataḥ syāt evañca śākhāntare’pyāha vāgyataḥ karmāṇi sāryamāṇa

diśā na vyaveteti tasmāt sarvatra brahmā dakṣiṇataḥ śrāvasatho’pi brahmaṇo
devayajanasya dakṣiṇata eva syāt tasmādyuta sarvagrahaṇam || 1 ||

syādi tadṛtvigbhiḥ prāśayeyuḥ tattasmāttandulānāhītvā apavidhyeyuḥ

athānyān tandalān jatāsvāśvatthīṣu samitsu prāyaḥ apare
bruvate tasminnevāgnā prakṣipeyuriti || 14 ||
ādhāsyamānasyāraṇyoḥ prattayo yathārthath syāt || 15 ||
yo’gmīnādhāyayitā sa ādhāsyamānaḥ tasyādhāsvamānasya ara
pyorarpita yoryathārthaṃ khāt yo yasyārthaḥ yathārthaḥ || 15 ||
pūrvāhṇe dakṣiṇenāgnyāyatanāni gatvā yatrāgniṃ manthiṣyantaḥ
syastaddakṣiṇato nirastaḥ prarāvasuriti dakṣiṇā tṛṇaṃ nirasyedā-
vasoḥ sadane sodāmotyupaviśet bhūbhuvaḥsvarvṛhaspatirbrahmācaṃ

moti prāyaścittamiti kiṃ prāyaścittamiti sarvaprāyacittamiti kiṃ
sarvaprāyaścittamiti mahāvyāhatoreva macavanniti yadi prāyaścittaṃ
nāma karmadoṣanidhānārthaṃ kriyate doṣe utpanne prāyaścittaṃ bhavati
tadyadi prāyaścittaṃ karttavyaṃ syāt bhūḥ svāheti gārhapatye juhuyāt
bhuvaḥ svāheti dakṣiṇamā yadi sutyā syādāgnītrīye khaḥ svāhe-
tyāhavanīye bhūrbhuvaḥsvaḥ svāheti tatraiva tatraiveti prakṛtāvadhāraṇaṃ
kriyate | nanu yadi prakṛtāvadhāraṇaṃ bhūrbhuvaḥkhaḥ svāhetyevameva
karttavyaṃ syāt atreocyate tatkecidvarṇayanti evaṃ kriyamāṇe bhū-
bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhetyetameva kevalāmājati syāt yā anyā vyāhatī
drāhmāyaṇo’pyevam

<<0431>> ṣaṣṭhaḥ prapāṭhakaḥ |
atha prathamā kaṇḍikā |
santani codyamānamekaikasyā sarva stomasambhavāta ||1||
ukta brahmatvaṃ sāmprataṃ mantanino vidhānamucyate kaḥ punarbrahmatvāna-
ntaraṃ mantanino’vasara iti ucyate udgācaṃ prakṛtaṃ tatra brahmatvaṃ prāsa-
ṅgikamukta sāmpratamayamācārya: sāmavidhānaṃ vakṣyati tacaikacaklaptiñca
tatra tasmin mantanini ṭcaikarcakriyāṃ prati saṃśayaḥ tatparīkṣārthaṃ santa-
nina eva tāvadvidhānamārabhate etat santanyāmnāye ṭace gītaṃ tatprayo-
gakāle ṭaceva manyate tadetaccinyate kimetadāmnāyagānaṃ pratyṛcaṃ sarvaṃ
kriyatāṃ atha yathāmnāyameveti kutaḥ saṃśayaḥ uccate pragīteṣu, darśitaṃ
santaninaskhayaḥ prastāvāḥ pradarbhyante yadyekasyāmmṛti sarvaṃ gīyate tata-
statprastāvanā sambhavati atha punaryathāmnāyaṃ tato’sya vākyasyānartha kya
bhavati cayaḥ prastāvasadṛśā iti śrata ārabhyate mantani codyamāna-
mekaikasyāṃ sarva stomasammavāditi santanīti māmnaḥ saṃjñā codyamānaṃ
ādiśyamānam ekaikasyāmmṛci sarvaṃ karttavyaṃ yadetat dvipadottare tayoreva
etaddvāname kaikasyāmmṛci sarva karttavyaṃ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ stomasambhavādeva evaṃ hi
kṛte slomaḥ sambhavati pañcabhaktiyuktena sānā stomaḥ saṃkhyāyate uktañca
* drāhmāyaṇenaitena sūtradvayaṃ kṛtam |

<<0432>> [6.1.4]
śrautasūtre |
prastāvodgotha pratihāropadravanidhanāni iti tadetā bhaktayaḥ kriyante
tataḥ stomaḥ sambhavati atha punarna kriyante tata utsṛṣṭaikadeśaṃ sāma kṛtaṃ
bhavati nacāyaṃ nyāyaḥ sāmaikadeśaiḥ stomasaṃkhyānamiti tasmādekaika
svāmmṛci sarvaṃ karttavyaṃ bhavati || 1
tathā cānyāni svavicchandaḥsu || 2 ||
tathā cānyāni sāmāni svacchandaḥsu vicchandaḥsu ca bhavanti
tathā tena prakāreṇetyarthaḥ vāravantīyayajñāyajñīyavāmadevyapañcanidhanavā-
madevyavat yathā vāravantīyamekasmin pāde kṛtsnaṃ paṭhitaṃ tathā yajñā-
yajñīyaṃ jagatīṣu gāyatrīṣu ca tathā vāmadevyaṃ gāyatrīṣu triṣṭapsu ca
gotaṃ tathā pañcanidhanaṃ vāmadevyam atiindaḥsu ca gītaṃ tathā kavatīṣu
gotaṃ rathantaram evametadgānamuttarābhyāṃ luptabhaktikaṃ dṛṣṭam || 2 ||
santanīti yadāhiṣṭhoyavata* || 3 ||
nanu yadyetatpratyṛcaṃ sarvaṃ gīyate tataḥ mantanitvannopapadyate yadi
bhaktāpāyaḥ kriyate tataḥ mantanilaṃ bhavati anyathā mantanitva na
bhavati anrocyate mantanīti yadāhiṣṭhīyavat yathā yadvāhiṣṭhīyaṃ
sṛte’pi yadāhiṣṭhaśabdāt yadvāhiṣṭhīyatvaṃ naiva jahāti evametatsantani
ṛte’pi bhaktilopāt santanitvaṃ na jahāti || 3 ||
triṣu vā ḍhaceṣvekacavattṛce darśanāta* || 4 ||

caḍhaktānāmā digrahaṇena vidhiranādeśe || 1 ||

prayogaṃ prati saṃśayaḥ kathaṃ prayoktavyānīti so’yamācāryasteṣāṃ prayoga-

deśe iti tṛcāśca sruktāni ca tisra ṛṛcaḥ ṭaca ityupacaryate satāni
catucaprabhṛtīni teṣāmādigrahaṇe kriyamāṇe samastasya vacasya
sṛtasya vā prayogaḥ syāt anādeśe yatra vādeśaḥ tatra yathādeśaṃ yathā

trayodaśatrayo viśayoḥ pañcavieśe ca madhyamaḥ paryāyo
jyāyānekajyāyaḥsu kanoyānekakanoyaḥ su* || 5 ||
trayodaśatrayoviṃśayoḥ stomayoḥ pañcaviṃśe ca stome viśeṣa
ārabhyate ekayā stotrīyayā jyāyaḥsu yo madhyamaḥ paryāyaḥ ma jyāyān
syāt ekayā kanīyaḥsu ekayā kanīyān madhyamaḥ paryāyaḥ svāt tat
kimidaṃ bahuvacanaṃ yadā ekaḥ kanīyān jyāyāṃ dau syātāṃ tatrai-
ke tāvadarṇayanti paryāyeṣu bahuvacanamiti ekojyāyān yeṣu paryā-
yeṣu time ekajyāyāṃsaḥ ekaḥ kanīyān yeṣu tadame ekakanīyāṃsaḥ
apare bruvate stomeṣveva bahuvacanaṃ yathā narāṇāṃ vā narāṇāñca katha-
māsot samāgamaḥ atriṣṭujagatokā asya stotrapravaḥ savanapravaḥ sya
athavā paryāyakṛtirevāsya prāthamyena vivacitā tatra cayodaśe tāvat
ekayājyāyami prathamottamā paryāyā dvādaśāt madhyamaḥ pañcadaśaśat
tathā pañcaviṃśe caturviṃśāt prathamottama paryāyo madhyamatriṇavāt
trayoviṃśa ekayā kanīyān tasmiṃścaturviṃśāt prathamottamā madhyama
ekaviṃśāt dhānaapyastu jātisaṃhāraṃ manyate ubhayorjātisaṃhāraṃ
dhānañjapya iti || 5 ||
tathaikānnatriśaikatriśayoḥ || 6 ||
tathā tena prakāreṇa jyāyaḥkanīyastvaṃ ekonatriṃśe prathamottamau
triṃśāt madhyamakhiṇavāt tathaikatriṃśe prathamottamo ciṃśāt madhyama-
strayastriṃśāt || 6 ||
* drāhmāyaṇopyevam |

śrautasūtre 15
mucyate evaṃ śrutiḥ atha khalvāśī: samṛddhirupasaraṇānītyadhikṛtya yāṃ
devatāmabhiṣṭoṣyaṃ syāt tāṃ devatāmupadhāvediti iha ca savanadevatā
ākuvādastotradevatā api śrūyate yathā vasūnāṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ rudrāṇaṃ
mādhyandinaṃ savanamādityānāñca viśveṣāñca devānāṃ tṛtīyasavanamiti
anyo jyotiṣe daivatayogaḥ tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ savanadevatā tenopa-
dikhate athavā stotradevatā śratha jyotiṣaṃ daivatayogaṃ gṛhītvopāsyā-
maha iti etasmin saṃśaya āha yaddevatyāsa stuvate sā stotradevateti
bhaktimātra savanadevatā || 4 ||
anvadhyāyamapavāda niśāmanam || 5 ||
ihe chandodaivatasāmāntayogān nyāyyān bruvate yathā
ghoड़śimato’tirātrasya jyotiṣṭomasyeti anyatrāgneyoṣu sarvāṇi
stotrāṇi bruvate yathāgniṣṭutsu aindroṣu bhavantīti sarvāṇi stotrāṇi
aindrīṣu bhavanti tathā vaiśvadevīṣu bhavantīti atyantaraṃ tatkimeṣāṃ
stotrāṇamāgneyyādiṣu kriyamāṇānāṃ yā eva stotradevatā nyāyyā
nirdiṣṭā jyotiṣṭome tā eva bhavanti agnyādayo guṇabhṛtāḥ yathendro
gārhapatyamupatiṣṭhata iti agnireva bhavati tatra prādhānyena tat śruteḥ
indro guṇabhṛtaḥ evaṃ tat yathāgnyādidevatābhiḥ tanyāyastotradevatānāṃ
pratyāmnāya iti etasmin saṃśaya āī anvadhyāyamapavādaniśāmana-
miti adhyāyamanu anvadhyāyaṃ anvadhyāyamapavādo niśāmayitavyaḥ
anvadhyāyaṃ nyāyyānāṃ chandodaivatasāmāntānāmapavādaḥ yathā vandamāṃ
drāhmāyaṇopyevam |

iha jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe devā vā agniṣṭomamabhijityākthāni

iti śraṣṭamasya dvitīyā kaṇḍikā |

yadā vidāhi sthaṇḍilam * || 5 ||
yasminnoṣadhayo vidahyante tadvidāhi etasmincā vidāhini stha-
ṇḍile devayajanaṃ kuryuḥ || 5 ||
śavanabhye adhiṣavaṇe iti yena yānena mmṛtaṃ nirvaheyustasya
nabhye adhiṣavaṇaphalake kuryuḥ | || 6 ||
drāhmāyaṇoṭapyevam |
|hāhyāyanaitena sūtradayaṃ kṛtam |

<<0586>> śrautasūtre |
brāhmaṇaṃ śavanabhye adhiṣavaṇa iti śavanabhya iti kimuktaṃ bhavati
ucyate yena yānena mṛtaṃ nirvaheyuḥ śavantasya yānasya nabhye nābhyā
nirvṛtte adhiṣavaṇaphalake kuryuḥ || 6 ||
571
acaṣālo yūpasphyāgraḥ || 7 ||
brāhmaṇaṃ tailvako vā bādhako vā yūpasphāgra iti tatra saṃśayaḥ
kathaṃ sphāāgra iti kiṃ syāgraḥ upamārtho’yamatha sphāgra evāgre
mo’yaṃ sphāāgra iti so’yamācārya āha acaṣālā yūpaḥ syāgra iti
nāstyasya caṣālamityacaṣāla iti || 7 ||
lohitoṣṇoṣā lohitavāsaso nivotā ṛtvijaḥ praca
reyurupotaparuṣā ujyadhanvānaḥ || 8 ||
brāhmaṇaṃ lohitoṣṇoṣā ityādi lohitānyuṣṇīṣāṇi yeṣānte
lohitoṣṇoṣāḥ uṣṇoṣāṇi śiraso veṣṭanāni vāsāṃsi teṣāñca
vāsamāṃ lohito varṇaḥ syāt nivītāḥ kaṇṭhālamvitasṛjā evaṃ lakṣa-
ṇāste pracareyuḥ karmāṇi kuryuḥ upotaparuṣāḥ āsannaparuṣāḥ paruṣā duva
vyavasthitāḥ apare bruvate upotāca paruṣāceti upotāḥ kañcukinaḥ
pūrva evetyarthaḥ ujyadhanvānaḥ udgata jyāmujyam udgatajyānyeṣāṃ dhanūṃṣi
bhavanti || 8 ||
pavamāne rathantaraṃ karotīti bṛhatyāmekacanāra sthāne
syādekaṃ taddhi bāītānāeṃ sthānamevañca ṭace bhavati || 8 ||
* drāhmāyaṇopyevam |
↑ brāhmāyaṇenaitena sūtradayaṃ kṛtam |

<<0587>> [8.5.12)
brāhmaṇaṃ pavamāne rathantaraṃ kuyāditi tat rathantaraṃ vṛhatyā-
mekarcānāṃ sthāne syāt vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanarauravayodhājayānāmekameteṣāṃ

<<0588>> śrautasūtre |
tyānuvādakhikaṃ stomaṃ dṛṣṭvā athāpūrvī vidhiriti kiṃ punariti yadi

apūrvo vidhiḥ tatra paratva kalpayitavyaṃ so’yamācārya āha pṛṣṭheṣu
rathantarasya kriyamāṇasya uttarayoḥ stotrīyayoḥ kakubhoḥ sthāne dvipade
syātāmityācāyāḥ evaṃ kriyamāṇe tāḥ sarvāḥ suṣṭutarāḥ parāyo
bhavantīti || 12 ||

|| 13 ||

<<0590>> śrautasūtre |

<<0591>> māyāyanīye
asminneva brāhmaṇa tā u catasraḥ sampadyanta iti cāturuttaryeṇa
stotrīyānte saptachandāṃsi sampadyante tāsāṃ sampaducyate tasmiṃścaturuttara-
sampanne i i trikapañcino stotre karttavye pratyavarāheṇa pratyavarohaḥ
prātilomyam upariṣṭādārabhya gāyatrīsampannastāvaduktaḥ sāmprataṃ tasmi-
nneva viśeṣa uccate uṣṇikusampanne ārbhavastrikaḥ pañcī agniṣṭomasāma
anena prakāreṇa pratyavarāhet yāvajjagatīsampannamiti || 25 ||
576
tasya ṣaṭṣaṣṭhaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇā: * || 26 ||

bṛhatīsampanne catuḥpañcāśaṃ śataṃ
paṅktisampanna pañcāśaṃ śataṃ triṣṭusampanna ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaṃ śataṃ jagato
sampanne dācatvāriṃśaṃ śatam evameṣā jyotiṣi stocīyāsampannasya na
bhavati śataṃ stotrīyā iti dakṣiṇābhiśca sampadyate || 26 ||

iti vyaṣṭamasya pañcamī kaṇḍikā |
atha ṣaṣṭhī kaṇḍikā |

<<0592>> śrautasūtre |
-
uktāḥ sādyaḥkrāḥ sāmprataṃ vrātyastomā uccante tān vivakṣuridaṃ
sūtramārabhate vrātyastomairiti vrātyānāṃ stomāḥ kiṃlakṣaṇāḥ puna-
vrītyā iti uccate paṭhitā brāhmaṇena honā vā ete hīyante ye vrātyāṃ
pravasanti na hi brahmacaryaṃ racanti na kṛṣiṃ na vaṇijyamiti tathā gara-
girā vā ete ye brahmādyaṃ janma mantramadantyaduruktavākyaṃ durutamārada-
eḍā daṇḍena ghnanta carantyaḥ dīkṣitā dīkṣitavācaṃ vadantīti evaṃprakārāḥ
vrātyāḥ paṭhitāḥ ye cānye śākhāntareṣu padyante te sarve vrātyāḥ vrātya-
stomairiti karaṇe tṛtīyā yakṣyamāṇa iti bhaviṣyatkālopadeśaḥ te
vrātyā vrātyastomairyacya māṇāḥ pṛthagagnīnādhāya pṛthaṅnānetyarthaḥ pṛtha-
gagnyādhānāni kṛtvā yajñopakaraṇāni ceṣṭā yajñopakaraṇāni yajñasādha-
nāni dravyāṇi arjayitvā ya eṣāṃ vrātyānāmadhyayane’bhikrāntitamaḥ
syāt abhikrāntā adhyayanena sarva ime abhikrāntinaḥ śrayameṣāmabhi-
katatama: taśayana tamataṭhat a va astaraca
abhijanaḥ kulaṃ yaḥ kulena vādhikaḥ syāt tadabhāve’pi bhogalābhena
tayorabhāvastadabhāvaḥ tayoḥ svādhyāyābhijanātirekyorasambhave bhoga-
lābhena ye’tiricyate dravyavattamaḥ syāt tasya gāīpate dokṣeran sa
teṣāṃ mukhyaḥ syāt bhakṣāṃśca tasyānu sarve bhakṣayeyuḥ || 1 ||
[8.6.2]
577
ye ke ca brātyāḥ sampādayeyuste prathamena yajeran * || 3 ||

<<0595>> lāyāyanīye
[8.6.12]
vipathaśva phalakāstīrṇa iti prācyaratho nāstīṇa vipathaḥ*
||8||
vipathaca phalakāstīrṇa iti brāhmaṇa tat ko vipathaḥ kathañca
phalakāstīrṇa iti ucyate vipathastāvat prācyarathaḥ utkramya panthānaṃ
yāti vipathaḥ anyadeva tasya mānaṃ phalakāstīrṇaḥ yathā patita eva
vaṃśaphalābhireva nāstīrṇa : na cānyenāstaraṇena sa viṣathaḥ || 8 ||
kampamiśrābhyāmaśvāśvatarābhyāṃ yuktaḥ syāditi śāṇḍi-
lyaḥ || 10 ||

maśvāśvatarābhyāṃ yuktaḥ svāt sa vipathaḥ kampanaśīlaḥ kampraḥ aśvaśva
aśvataraca aśvāśvatarī tayorekaḥ kampanaśīlaḥ kañcana tābhyāmavaśya-
mevotpathaḥ kriyate gativaiṣamyāt evamasau vipatho bhavati || 10 ||
yābhyāṃ kābhyācā śvābhyāmaśvatarābhyāṃ veti dhānañjapyaḥ +
580
||11||

brāhmaṇaṃ kṛṣṇaśaṃvāsaḥ kṛṣṇabalate ajine rajato niṣkastadgṛhapate-

tatra tasmintīvrasuti ye bhakṣā māmnātāḥ tayā vṛtāḥ tenaiva
vidhinetyarthaḥ camamānavajighrayuḥ avajighraṇamātra kuryu: bhakṣayeyuḥ yasmā-
dāi abhakṣayanta ṛtvijañcamasānavajighrantīti tāṃcāchāvākasya stotre
stutvā bhakṣayeyuḥ yasmādevaṃ brāhmaṇamāha tānachāvākasya stotre bhakṣa-
yantīti || 10 ||
eva sarveṣu savaneṣu | || 11 ||
anena prakāreṇa sarveṣu savaneṣu camamānāṃ bhakṣaṇavidhiḥ || 11 ||

|| 12 ||

† drāhmāyaṇo’pyevam kintu tatra chedaviṣaye viśeṣo’sti |

<<0623>> [8.11.1]

somaṃ miśraṃ kuryuryathā vaiśyastome || 13 ||
*

prātaḥsavane paṭatena madhyandine danā tṛtīyasavane || 13 ||

hyāha* || 14 ||

iti kāṣṭamasya daśamī kaṇḍikā |

<<0627>> lāthāyanīye
[8.11.18]
ekekasya pṛthakvena varaṇaṃ kuryāt atharliggrahaṇaṃ kimarthamiti

rājā rājadayena yajeta* || 1 ||
uko vājapeyaḥ anantaraṃ rājayo vaktavyaḥ taṃ vivakṣurārabhate

tiṣṭomāya* || 2 ||
phalgunībhyāṃ yuktā phālgunī phālagunyāḥ pataḥ phālgunīpakṣaḥ
tasya phālgunopatkṣaya yā prathamā tithistasyāṃ dīkṣeta abhyārohaṇīyāya
jyotiṣṭomāya uktam agniṣṭomaṃ prathamamāharatītyādi maśakenāpyukta
klṛpto jyotiṣṭoma iti so’bhyārohaṇaṇeyāya jyotiṣṭomaḥ syāt tasmai
tadarthaṃ dīkṣeta || 2 ||
tasyaikā dīkṣā dvādaśaśataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ || 3 ||
tasya abhyārohaṇīyastha jyotiṣṭomasyaikā docā syāt dvādaśaṃ

saṃvatsarādūī keśavapanīyāya dokṣeta yasmin kāle’bhiṣeca

ukta daśapeyaḥ tasyāvaṭathādudetya saṃvatsarandevavratāni carediti
tatastasmāt saṃvatsarādū keśavapanīyāya dīkṣata keśavapanīya iti
saṃjñā saṃvatsaraṣṭatānāṃ keśānāṃ tasmin vapanaṃ kriyate keśavapanīyāyeti
tādarthye caturthī dīkṣa teti yajamānasya kriyopadeśaḥ yasmin kāle-
’bhiṣecanīyena yajeteti abhiṣecanīyasya kāla uktaḥ || 1 ||
tasya paurṇamāsyāmatirātraḥ || 2 ||
*

syāditi || 3 ||

honāḥ matrāṇīti śrayaṃ niścayaḥ jyotiṭomātirātrādayaḥ ete

ye ca na sarveṣāmahīnaśabdaḥ sāmānyaḥ śrutiprāmāṇyāt jyotiṣṭomā-

śrautasūtre |
nivṛttā tadāhonikya mati ko viśeṣaḥ myāditi uccate upasada-
svāvadāhonikyaḥ syuḥ ṣaṇāṃ sambhavo’sti evaṃ kṛtvā nidānakāropi
middhamahīnevvityupakramya keśavapanīyaprakaraṇamāha prācīnastoma uttaraḥ
ityevamadhikṛtya athāpīdaṃ dvitīyaṃ yajñasthānaṃ yadahīno dvitīyo varṇaḥ
kṣatriya iti || 6 ||
645
tatprabhṛtīnāṃ bhūyasyaḥ satyābhyuccayena* || 7 ||

satyābhyutayena yathā yathā sutyā varddhayeran tathā tathā dakṣiṇa varddha-
yeran kaḥ punarupajanaḥ syāditi ucyate dau nyāyau dṛṣṭau ekastrai-
rātrikaḥ prativināśo dṛṣṭaḥ trayastriṃśaca trīṇi ca śatāni prathame’hani
deyāstathā dvitīye tathā tṛtīye tathānukāravacane atha caturthādi-
svapi pratisutyaṃ aparonyāyaḥ yathā dīyamānāsu pauṇḍarīke ayuta-
mupapadyate tathopajanaṃ kuryyāditi pañcaviṃśa śataṃ sahasrañcopajana iti
ekā evamayutotpattiḥ pauṇḍarika iti || 7 ||
tāḥ sama sarveṣvahaḥsu vibhājaṃ dadyāt ||| 8 ||
vibhajya vibhajya vibhājam || 8 ||
samānupapattāvuttame’hani bhūyiṣṭhāḥ || 8 ||

<<0661>> lāyāyanīye
ayutamekādaśarātre dadyāt || 10 ||
ekādaśarātre pauṇḍarīke ayutaṃ dadyāt nanu tatkimidamārabhyate

nava nava pūrveyvaha su śatāni sahasramuttame || 11 ||
navanavaśatāni pūrveṣvahaḥsu prathamādiṣu yāvaddaśamamiti uttame
ekādaśe sahasraṃ dadyāt tatra hi yaddaśamamadhikaṃ śataṃ tatra samaṃ pravi-
bhāgaṃ karttu mekādaśasu grahaḥsu nava nava bhavanti ekāvaśiṣyate mā utta
me’hani dīyate evaṃ pravibhāgo mābhūdityata āha yadyevaṃ nava nava pūrveṣva-
haḥsu śatānīti ukte mahasramavaśiṣyate taduttama eva dāsyate tatkimi-
damārabhyate sahasra muttama iti uccate uttame’hani dādaśāhe upajana-
nyāyena dakṣiṇāvibhāgāḥ prāptāḥ tāṣu prāptāsvāha mahasramuttama iti
uccate naitadyutaṃ pradhāne jñāpakajñāpitā dakṣiṇa iti na yuktā janyāḥ

kālā vāk || 7 ||

ekastomānāmanati tathā trayastrivṛto tirātrāḥ sarve ṣoड़śimanta
iti vaidacirātre śrutiḥ tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimayamahaḥstomo vidhīyate

sarātrikāṇyahāni tatstomānyeveti etasmin saṃśaye trācārya:

<<0695>> lāthāyanī ye

svatantrātveva syuḥ kṛtalakṣaṇā hi purastāccodyante pratyakṣa-
vikārāta stomacodanā catuṣṭomasarvastomayoḥ || 14 ||
680
śratha yaduta yathā catuṣṭomasarvastomayoḥ pratyakṣaśiṣṭayoḥ stoma
codanāmātraṃ bhavati evameteṣāṃ stomacodanāmātra syāt kiṃ kāraṇaṃ
yasmāt trirātreṣu ca tantravilopo na vidyata iti tanna natvevaṃ syāt
tuśabda: pūrvapakṣanivṛttyarthaḥ yaduka teṣāṃ stomacodanaiva syāditi
tantra svatantrā eva syuḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yammāt purastāt kṛtalakṣaṇa hi
caudyante teṣāṃ kṛtalakṣaṇaṃ na caudyamānānāṃ stomacodanāmātra pratī-
yāt atha caduktaṃ yathā catuṣṭomasarvastomayorityatra brūmaḥ pratyakṣa-
vikārāt catuṣṭomasarvastomayoḥ stomacodanāmātra pratīyate pratyakṣa
vikāraḥ kṛta eva maśakena || 14 ||
vacanāttantravilopo yathā jāmikarūpaḥ sarvasvāre || 15 ||
atha yaduktaṃ trirātreṣu ca tantravilopo na vidyata ityatra brūmaḥ
tantravilopo vacanādbhavati vacanaṃ balīyaḥ na hi tadasti yadvacanānna
bhavati pratyacaśiṣṭatvāt jyotiṣṭomādīnāṃ śrutyantare || 15 ||

trayodaśyāmaparapakṣasya dokṣeta jāmadagnāya* || 1 ||
aśvamedha uktaḥ anantaraṃ vaidacirātrādayaḥ paribhāṣāmiddhāḥ

miti tithinirdeśaḥ aparapakṣasyeti sāmānyavidhiprāptasya pūrvapakṣasya
pratyāmnāyaḥ dīneteti kriyānirdeśa: jāmadagmāyeti jāmadamārthaṃ
tāda caturthī eṣa sūtrārtha: jāmadagrena catūrātreṇa yakṣyamāṇa-
khayodaśyāmaparapakṣasya dīkṣeta || 1 ||

lomā dvādaśakapālādayaḥ ekakapālāntāḥ na mantraiḥ prātilomyam
śrayaṃ dīkṣopasanniyamo viṃśatiḥ dīkṣā dvādaśopasada iti sampadarthaḥ
utaṃ hyasya brāhmaṇe jagatī cchadobhiḥ sampadyata iti na dīkṣābhirupamadbhiḥ
upariṣṭāt dvādaśabhiriṣṭibhiḥ jagatī sampadyate kathaṃ purāड़āśairupamatsa
ca caturviṃśatiranyāskhiṣṭiṣu caturviṃśatyeva jagatī sampadyate || 7 ||
vasiṣṭhasya janitre bhavata iti samarpasya caturtho’hani
bṛhatyanuṣṭubhoḥ pṛthaganupūrvamanukalpayeccaturthaś hi janitra-
sthānam || 8 ||
uktaṃ vasiṣṭhasya janitre bhavata iti te kalpayatyācāryaḥ maṃsarpasya
kratāḥ caturthe’hani bṛhatyanuṣṭubhoḥ pṛthaṅgānā anupūrvam anukalpa-
yet bṛhatyāṃ pūrvam anuṣṭubhi uttaraṃ yasmācaturthamaharjanitrasya
sthānam || 8 ||
tayeorvikalpaḥ syādārṣeyakalpena | || 9 ||

sthāt na tayorniyamaḥ || 8 ||

pakṣeṣu + || 10 ||

tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ ke’trālabdhavyāḥ ke cotsṛthvyā iti tadayamācāryo

vyati || 11 ||

(8.12.16)
ṣaṣyāṃ śaradi kārttike māsi yajeta* || 13 ||
pañcasu saṃvatsareṣu gateṣu yā ṣaṣṭho śarat tatyāṃ kārttike māmi
pañcaśāradīyena yajeta || 13 ||
tasya dvādaśopasadaḥ || 14 ||
685
tasya pañcaśāradīyasya dvādaśopamadaḥ syuḥ ṣaड़iti dhānañjayaḥ
ityetannivarttayati || 14 ||
tṛtoye ṣaḍḍātre pañcamasyāhaḥ pratyavarohīṇyukthāni syu
rityācāyī abhyāsaṃgyohyatra yathā devānāṃ pañcarātre ||15||
dau ṣaड़hau paribhāṣitā krato ṣaड़ha āyuḥkāmaṣaड़hañca
tṛtīye kiñciddhivacitaṃ taducyate tatra paṭhati abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāha
iti toye ṣaड़āne pañcamasyā pratyavare hī yukthāni syuriti
evamācāyā manyante kasmāt yasmādatrābhyāmodyate yathā devānāṃ
pañcarātre tatra pañcame’hani pratyavarāhakthāni tasmādiddāpi tathaiva
syāt abhyāsaṅkhyātideśāt || 15 ||
rātrikāritastatra pratyavaroha iti gautamastrayastriṃśā-
nyeva syuriti + || 16 ||

tatkāritastatra pratyavarohaḥ dūha punaḥ pañcamamahaḥ ukthasaṃstham eva bhavati
tasmāt tatra trayastriṃśānyeva syuriti yātu pratyavarāhasya nimitta
rātriḥ sā viśvajiti kariṣyati tatra pratyavarāho bhaviṣyati || 16 ||
686
saptarātrāṇāṃ prathamasthātirātra eka viśānyakthāni

saptarātrāṇāṃ prathame paṭhati pṛthyaḥ ṣaड़hā mahāvratamatirātra iti
tatrāyaṃ maṃśayaḥ mahāvrate kimukyāni vratastomamanuvarttatām athaika-
viṃśastomāni bhavanti etasmin saṃśaye ayamācārya prārabhate saptadaśa-

<<0702>> daśamaḥ prapāṭhakaḥ |
atha prathamā kaṇḍikā |
dokṣākrayaprasavotthānāni sarvasatreṣu pūrvapakṣa upapāda-
yeyuḥ || 1 ||
ahonānantaraṃ satrāṇi vaktavyāni tāni vivakṣurācārthya: pari-
bhāṣāmārabhate dokṣākrayaprasavotthānāni sarvasatreṣu pūrvapakṣupapā-
dayeyuriti dokṣā ca krayaśca prasavaśca utthānañca docākrayaprasavo-
tthānāni tasminnahani dīkṣeran yathaitāni sarvāṇi pūrvapakṣe bhavanti
sarvaśabdo niravaśeṣavācī || 1 ||
teṣāmekasyānupapattā krayo’parapakṣaṃ syāt * || 2 ||
teṣāṃ dīkṣādīnāmekasyānupapattau krayaḥ aparapace syāt anupa-
pattirasāmarthya kālasya sampādane || 2 ||
prasavaśca yadi dve* || 3 ||
yadi ho na sambhaveyātāṃ prasavañca aparapace syāt krayaśca iti
prakṛtam || 3 ||
drāhmāyaṇopyevam |

<<0703>> lāthāyano ye
ciṣūtyānameva pūrvapakṣaṃ syāt * || 4 ||
triṣvanupapadyamāneṣu utthānameva pūrvapakṣe sthāt eṣāmudāharaṇa-
mātramucyate kṣullake dvādaśāhe tathā viśvasṛjāmayane saptatriṃśat-
samākhye catvāri syuḥ yathākramaṃ kṣullakatāpañcite tāvadokṣākrayaprasavo-
tthānāni sarvāṇi paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pūrvapane upapadyante dādaśāhe
pūrvapakṣasya saptamyāṃ dīkṣitvā dvādaśadīkṣāstataḥ aparapakṣasya caturthā
krayaḥ sampadyate evaṃ dīkṣākrayaprasavotyānāni cīṇi pūrvapakṣaṃ sampa
dyante viśvasṛjāmayane pūrvapakṣasya ṣaṣṭhyāṃ dīkṣitvā parapakṣasya tṛtī-
yāyāṃ krayaḥ sampadyate śramāvasyā prasave mahalasaṃvatsara iti saptatriṃśadrā-
ceṣu vratavatsu sarveṣvamāvāsyāyāṃ dīkṣitvā tasmin kāle maha sṛtyābhiḥ
ṣaड़hāni sambatsarādadhikāni kṛtvottiṣṭheyuriti śramāvāsyāyāṃ
dīkṣitānāṃ dīkṣākrayaprasavā aparapakṣa bhavanti utthānameva kevala
pūrvapace sampadyate || 4 ||

(10.1.6]

<<0704>> śrautasūtre |
dhānañjapya
sāṃvatsarikebhyaśca satrebhya ūīṃ dīkṣāṇaṃ yathākāmī syāt yā-
thākāmyamiṣṭataḥ pravṛttiḥ sāṃvatsarikāni gavāmayanādīni satrāṇi || 6 ||
prathame pañcadaśarātra ekānnaviṃśatikṣā iti dhānañjapya
ekāṣṭakā mahāvratamamāvāsyātirātra iti hyāheti || 7 ||
prathame pañcadaśarātre ekānnaviṃśatiḥ dīkṣāḥ syuḥ ityevaṃ
ācārya āha evaṃ hi brāhmaṇamāha ekāṣṭakāmahāvratamamāvāsyāti
rātra iti evaṃ kriyamāṇe eṣa kalpaḥ sampadyate paiaurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ
ekānnaviṃśatiḥ dokṣāḥ kṛtvā pūrvapakṣasya caturthī krayaḥ tataḥ aparapakṣasya
pratipadyatirāja kṛtvā ṣaड़haṅkṛtvā aṣṭamyāṃ mahāvrataṃ tataḥ punaḥ ṣaड़haṃ
kṛtvā śramāvāsyāyāmatirātraḥ || 7 ||
[10.1.8]
aṣṭādaśeti gautamaḥ paurṇamāsyatirāca iti hyāceti ||8||
gautama śrācārya śraha aṣṭādaśadīkṣāḥ syuriti yasmādevaṃ brāhmaṇa-
māha paurṇamāsyatirātra iti atrāpi paurṇamāsyāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ
aṣṭādaśadīcāḥ kṛtvā tṛtīyāyāṃ pūrvapattasya krayo bhavati tataḥ paurṇa-
māsyāṃ prāyaṇīyo’tirātraḥ tataḥ ṣaड़haṃ kṛtvā saptamoṃ laṅghayitvā
aṣṭamyāṃ mahāvrataṃ kṛtvā śramāvāsyāyāmatirājaḥ natveṣanyāyo yuktaḥ na
hi laṅghanamaho yukta mantānavirodhāt tasmāt nyūnamaparapakṣaṃ vidhāya
kalpaṃ kuryyāt || 8 ||

[10.2.2]
atha dvitīyā kaṇḍikā |
śarkaroṣu ṣoड़śinā stuvīteti gaurīvitaṃ mahānāmnīṣu
syāhakacodanā hi tatpra karaṇe* || 1 ||
ṣoड़śiprakaraṇe caturthe’hani paṭhati gaurīvitamadhikṛtya śarvarīṣu
ṣoड़ śinā stuvīteti tatrāyaṃ saṃśayaḥ kimatra śarkarthya: gaurīvitasya
ṛcaścodyanta śratha sāmacodanaiveyam iti kutaḥ punarayaṃ saṃśayaḥ cāda-
nāt eva śarkarīṣu ṣoड़śinā stuvateti adhikaraṇe paṇa saptamī
śrūyate śarvvarīṣu ṛkṣu gaiaurovitena sāmnā stuvīranniti atha dṛṣṭā
etā mahānāmnatraḥ ghoड़śisāmeti kṛtvā agniḥ sāmaceodaneti ṛbhi
rāśrayeṇa māna śrāśrayeṇa ca codaneti maṃśaye trācārya idaṃ sūtramā-
rabhate śarīṣu ṣoड़ śinā stuvīteti yadetadbrāhmaṇaṃ tatra gaurīvitaṃ
mahānāmnīṣu ṛtu syāt kiṃ kāraṇaṃ tasya prakaraṇe yasmādṛkaco-
danā || 1 ||
mahānāmanyastveva ṣoड़śisāma syurna hotāsvanyatsāmāpa-
dyate || 2 ||
*
tuśabda: pakṣanivṛtyarthaḥ yadukkaṃ gaurīvitaṃ mahānāmnīṣu svāditi
tantra mahānāmmā eva ghoड़śimāma syuḥ yasmādetāsu na kadācidapi
anyatmāmāpadyate anyāsa ṛtu dṛśyante anyāni sāmāni āpadya-
mānāni etāsu na kadācidapyanyatmāmāpadyate || 2 ||
* drāhmāyo naitena sūtradayaṃ kṛtam |

uttamayā stotrīyayā saṃyukta puroṣamānantaryāditi dhāna-
apya: * || 10 ||
tisraḥ stotrīyāḥ paṭhitvā purīṣaṃ paṭhati tatkiṃ purīṣa mahā-
nāmmīṣu sakṛtprayoktavyam śratha pṛthageva taditi uccate uttamayā

mayā saha yujyeta yāvatkṛtva uttamatā prayujyate tāvatkṛtvaḥ purīṣāṇi
prayujyante || 10 ||
śarkarobhiḥ stutvetyapavarjya puroṣeṇetyāca tasmādasaṃyuktaṃ
syāt + || 11 ||

<<0721>> 706.
[10.4.4]
na hi pṛthṣyaḥ stomaḥ prakṛtiḥ ucyate pṛthyapañcāhā evāsya vivakṣitāḥ
bṛhadrathantaraṣṭaṣṭhyatāmabhipretya samūḍhañca pṛṣyastomena pradeśaṃ karoti yadi
tu pṛśyena pradeśaṃ kuyāt pṛthyāni pramajyeran vyūḍha़ samūḍha़tāyā ca
vikalpa: syāt evaṃ mābhūdityataḥ pṛthyastomena pradiśati pṛthya eva
tvasya prakṛtitvenābhipretaḥ viśvajidancavāyāt iha ca manyāmahe pṛthya-
stomapañcāhā iti yenaiva viśvajidanvavaiti ya ete pṛthyavilāpā
etān sarvān viśvajidanvavaiti tathā ḍhatīye ṣaḍāce abhyāsaṅgyaḥ
pañcāhā viśvajidatirātraḥ tathā dvitīye navarātre jyotiṣṭomo’gni-
ṭomo gaurukthya āyurukthyo’bhyāsaṅkhyaḥ pañcāhā viśvajidatirātra
iti daśarātre’bhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāhāśvān vā yañchandomā viśvajidatirātra
iti eteṣāṃ pṛthyavilopaṃ kṛtvā viśvajidanvavāyo bhavati pṛṣṭhyānu-
grahārthaṃ nānā brahmasāmatvācca manyāmahe pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti na hi
nānā brahmasāma abhiśavaḥ śyaitanaudhasabrahmasāmatvāt tena pradeśaḥ
mānā brahmasāmānyupayantīti nityānuvādo’yaṃ yadi hyapūrvo bhavet
vidhirevābhaviṣṭat vidhāyakena vākyena vyavāyaḥ syāt nānā brahma-
sāmānyupeyuriti ṣaṣṭhasyālopavacanāt itaca manyāmahe pṛthyastoma
pañcācā iti yasmāt pṛthyaṃ prati ṣaṣṭhaskhālopavacanaṃ lupyate vā etat

jyotigarāyurityanādeśāt yadyasthābhitavikaḥ pañcāi iṭo bhavati
lādyāyanīye

<<0722>> [10.4.5]
śrautasūtre |
tatropadiśyate vātirātrojyotigarāyugarāyuḥ
pañcāha iti ica
punastasthānādeśāt manyāmahe pṛvyastomapañcāhā iti trivṛtā prayanti
citrodyantoti cāha evaṃ brāhmaṇamāha nivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodya-
ntīti tasya trittomaṃ prathamamahaḥ śrāvṛttasya tadevāhanīyaṃ bhavati
evametairhetubhirmanyāmahe pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iti || 4 ||
samāvete* || 5 ||
samāmlete hetavaḥ ya ete pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhale hetava uktāstān
samīkariṣyāmaḥ tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣanivṛtyartha: yaduktaṃ pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā
iti tanna ya evaite hetava uktā ubhayatraite samāḥ pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāheṣva-
bhivapañcāheṣu ca yattāvadutam anādeśe prakṛtipratyayādityatra brūmaḥ
naiva pṛṣṭhyaḥ stomaḥ prakṛtiḥ yaduktaṃ tvayā pṛthyamabhipretya pṛṣṭhyastomena pradi-
śatyetatropapadyate kathaṃ hi pṛṣṭhyomapañcāhā ityuke pṛṣṭhyasto mapañcāhā
iti pratoyeran tadyathaiva pṛṣṭhyastomasya dāsarātrikānyahāni prakṛti-
revamabhitavasyāpi tānyeva prakṛtiḥ tasmādanādeśe prakṛtipratyayā-
diti ubhayatrāyaṃ samāhetuḥ ubhāveto ṣaड़hāva bhilavapṛṣṭhyasto mau
vikṛtī tasmādubhayordaśāhikaḥ ṣaड़haḥ prakṛtiḥ atha yadukta viśva-
jidanvavāyādityatra brūmaḥ nātra pṛṣṭhānāṃ vilopoyadarthaṃ viśvajidanva-
vaitīti atra hi daśarātra prayogo vacyate tatprayogādeva pṛṣṭhānāma-
vilopaḥ na cāpi pṛṣṭhārthena viśvajidāgacchati viṣuvadarthenā-
gacchati atraṃ viśvajit tato ayamapi samāhetuḥ atha yadukta nānā
* brāhmāyaṇopyevam |

<<0723>> kāyāyanīce
[10.4.6]
brahmamāmalādana brūmaḥ nātra nānābrahmamāmānīti anityārthavādaḥ
apūrvameva nānā brahmasāmava vidhīyate nityānuvādava dvidhānāni
dṛśyante yathā rathantaraṃ bhavati cārca cāsmai daṇḍaṃ prayacchanvācayediti
atha yadukta pṛṣṭhyataḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāle| pavacanāditi atrāpyucyate yathaiva
pṛṣṭyastomasya bṛhadrathantarapṛṣṭhasya mataḥ ṣaṣṭhamaharlupyate evamevābhi-
lavasthāpi tasmāt samānolopaḥ ṣaड़hatantre atha yadukta jyoti-
gaurāyurityanādeśādityatra brūmaḥ yatra hyasya pṛṣṭhyastomapañcāhā iṣṭāḥ
tatrāpyādiśatyeva yathā pṛṣṭhyasya na labdhiḥ abhyāsaya pañcāha iti
yathā dvitīye navarātre daśarātre chando bhavati tadyathaivātra jyoti-
gaurāyurityanādeśe iti evaṃ pṛṣṭhyasto me’pyanādeśa iti yaduktaṃ citā
prayanti trivṛtodyantīti cāheti yatra brūmaḥ śrayaṃ trivṛchandaḥ na
kevalaṃ stomavācīti tritvañcāpekṣya bhavati yathā agninā pṛthivyau-
ṣadhibhistenāyaṃ lokastridṛt tathā agne vivasvaduṣama iti sandhinā
tu rityadhikṛtya cikaṃ stomaṃ vidhāyāha prāṇāvai trivṛtstomānā-
miti evamayaṃ trivṛcchandastrivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodyantīti uttame ca
jayattriṃgadrātre jilamiha samākhyābhipravarttate trivṛtā prayanti
trivṛtodyantīti purastātrayaḥ pañcāhāstraya upariṣṭāditi tasmādaya-
mapi heturubhayatra samaḥ ata ete hetavaḥ samīkṛtāḥ pratyuktā: rūpakṣa-
midānoṃ sthāpayiṣyāmaḥ || 5 ||
abhivapaścācā eveti gautame’dhikṛto hi sa satreṣu
bhavatītaraścādṛṣṭaḥ|| 6 ||
* brāhmāyaṇenatena sūtradayaṃ kṛtam |

<<0724>> [15.3.6]
śrautasūtre |
gautama trācārya śrāha abhiśavapañcāhā eva bhavantīti eva śabdo-
avadhāraṇartha: abhiśavapañcāhā eva na pṛṣṭhāstomapañcāhā iti yasmā-
dadhikṛtaḥ satreṣa abhiśavapañcāhaḥ atirātro jyotirgaurāyuḥ pañcāha
iti yarutamanādeśe prakṛtipratyayāditi anādeśajātireṣā bhavati
yadadhikāraḥ kiñcānyat dūtarañcādṛṣṭaḥ itaraca pṛthyastomapañcāhaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ
satreṣu kiṃ dṛṣṭārthaḥ pratīyatāmadṛṣṭārthaḥ pratoyatāmiti dṛṣṭapratyayo
nyāyata iti || 6 ||
abhyāsañcāsya prākṛtasyāpi kutaḥ pañcāsya* || 7 ||
abhyāsañcādṛṣṭaḥ prākṛtasya tāvat pṛṣṭhyasto masyaiva kutaḥ pañcāhasthā-
bhyāsaḥ syāditi yāvatā nidānakāro’pyāha prathāpi kṛtsnāveva
pṛṭhyaste|mau nābhiprayogaṃ labhete kuto viluptau labheyātāmiti || 7 ||
jyotigarāyugarāyuḥ pañcāhaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīya
iti ca parabrāhmaṇam | || 8 ||
yadapyukta jyotirgaurāyurityanādeśāditi iva pareṣāṃ brāhaṇa
jyotirāyugarāyuḥ sa dvitīyaḥ ma tṛtīya iti || 8 ||
eṣa pratnāvārkajambha vā pratipañcāhaṃ yathā lokabṛhadratha-
ntarāścet || 8 ||
ete pañcāhā bhavanti tata eṣa pratnā vā anurūpaḥ pratipañcā
vārkajambhaṃ vā prathame’hani || 8 ||
* drāhmāyaṇo’pyevam |
drāhmāyaṇīye viśeghoṭasti |

<<0725>> lāyāyanī ye
[10.4.14]

rabhibhiḥ || 10 ||

iti || 11 ||

saṃvatsara sammitāsu prathamaṃ dāśarātrikaṃ prāyaṇīyara svā-
dityeke trivṛdeva kāryyamiti hyāceti || 1 ||
saṃvatsarasaṃmitāsu paṭhatiṃ tadāhuryaccaturviṃśamahaḥ prāyaṇīyaṃ kuryyaḥ
saṃvatsaramārabhya na samāpayeyuriti trivṛdeva kāryamiti tatra kimidaṃ
trivṛtā liṅgena dāśarātrikaṃ prathamamahaśyodyete athavā tata adhikṛta-
syaiva prāyaṇīyasya stomavikāra dūti so’yametasminnarthe śāstramārabhate
saṃvatsarasaṃmitāsvityādi saṃvatsarasaṃmitā iti saṃjñā tāsu maṃvatsara-
saṃmitāsu prathamamahaḥ dāśarātrikaṃ prāyaṇīyaṃ syādityeke trācā vyā
ūcuḥ yasmādevaṃ brāhmaṇamāha trideva kāryya miti || 1 ||
prāyaṇoyantu codayitvā tasya stomavikāraṃ gṛhṇāti* ||2||

vidhānante pragāthā abhīvarttastotrīyāḥ syuḥ kiṃ viṣayasyābhovarttasya

kutaḥ punasta pragāthā āhartavyā iti ucyate catuḥśatamaindrā

nāḥ || 4 ||

lāthāyanīye
[10.6.8]
teṣāṃ sātābāītānāṃ cānāṃ ekaikaṃ tṛtīye tṛtīye’hani kuyāt
abhiśaveṣu prathamadvitīyatṛtīya caturthapañcamaṣaṣṭheṣu pragāthā na kṛtā hi
matāvṛhatyaḥ tṛtīye’hanyārṣeyakalpena śrālā sahasramāśatamityetāḥ
||7||
pañcamasya māsasyottame’bhipśave pañcame’hani satobṛhatoḥ
kuryāt pragāthā prabhavāt || 8 ||
pañcamasya māsasya ya uttamo’bhiśavastasminneva pragātho na
saṃpūryyate pañcame’hani matobṛhato: kuyāt dvau sātobṛhatau bacau
catvāraca pragāthāḥ evamekaviṃśatiḥ mātohahatyaḥ prayuktāḥ pragāthāca
sarve aṣṭo sātābāītāstṛcāḥ avaśiṣyante || 8 ||
teyvāpteṣu chandamī saṃyujyaitavyamiti ṣaṣṭhe māsi gāyatrī-
pādame kai kamuṣṇihāmu pariṣṭāt kuryādiṣṭāvānupapattirhyanyathā
uktaṃ pañcasu māḥsu bārhatāḥ pragāthā trāpyante tevvāpteṣu chandasi
saṃyujyaitavyantisṛṣu uṣṇihaḥ syurekā gāyatrī tāstisro bṛhatyo
bhavantīti yāvat teṣu pragātheṣu āpteṣu sarveṣu chandamī saṃyujyaitavya-
miti brāhmaṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsi gāyatrīpādamekaikamuṣṇahāmupariṣṭāt

drukāñcatuḥṣaṣṭhaṃ śatamabhilavānāṃ daśarātro vratamiti etadakṣaḥ sahasa
trikadrukā jyotirgaurāyuriti catuḥṣaṣṭhyadhikaṃ śataṃ abhilavānāṃ daśa-
rātrovratamiti || 13 ||
iti daśamasya caturdaśī kaṇḍikā |
traya pañcadaśī kaṇḍikā |
dakṣiṇe tīre sarasvacā vinaśanasya dīkṣeran sārakhatāya
paṇyāmpa tasyeti gautamaḥ || 1 ||
755
sahasrasāvyamuktam anantaraṃ sārasvatānyucyante tatra brāhmaṇaṃ mara-
svatyā vinaśane dīkṣeta iti yasmit deśe sarasvatyantarbhavati taddina-
śanamityucyate tasya vinaśanasya dakṣiṇe kūle tīre sārasvatāya tāda
caturthī ṣaṭhyāṃ tiyā pataya paribhāṣitam udagayanapūrvapacapuṇyāha-
miti gautama ācārya āha || 1 ||
amāvāsyāyāmatirātraḥ syādeva svasthānamāmāvāsyaṃ prayu-
jyate || 2 ||

brāhmāyaṇena sūtradayena sūtratrayaṃ kṛtam |

<<0771>> [10.15.5]
uktaṃ yadaharatirātro bhavati tadirvatmānapākurvanti saṃsthite’ti-

atirātrasyaiva kālo jñāpyate vatmāpākaraṇaṃ hi amāvāsyāyāṃ bhavati
tadanantare’hani sānnāyyena yāgaḥ so’yaṃ gautama śrācārya śrāha śramā-
vāsyāyāmatirātraḥ syādevaṃ svasthānamāmāvāsyaṃ prayujyata iti śrāmā-

<<0793>> nāthāyanīce
[10.20.3)
daṇḍa pāṇā kṛtvā pañcākāīpatyasyopaviśya svayaṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ
pratiṣajetam || 2 ||
ṣaṣṭhayāṃ tithau caitrīpakṣasya citrābhiryuktā paurṇamāmī caitrī yadetat
karma vadayate etat ṣaḍyāṃ caitrīpacasyārabhya kuyāt pañcamyāmiti
gautama trācārya śrāha pañcamyāṃ caitrīpacasya vratopāyanīyamodana-
maśilā środanaṃ bhukkā vratamupaiti yena taṃ vratopāyanīyamodanamopa-
varmāthakaṃ haviṣyamantraṃ bhukkā keśān śmaśrūṇica vāpayitvā ahataṃ vasanaṃ
paridhāva tāntukamanirṇikamaprāvṛtapūrvaṃ tahasanaṃ paridhāya parisamucyā
gmona paristortha tretāgnīnāṃ paristaraṇamādhvaryyave siddhaṃ praṇītāḥ praṇīya
praṇītāsaṃjñā mantrasaṃskṛtā āpaḥ mekhalāmābadhya mehanasya khalasya
mālā mekhalā adharottara kāyavibhāgārthā raśanetyarthaḥ muñjādīnāṃ
dravyāṇaṃ ekena nirvṛttā daṇḍa pāṇī kṛtvā pālāśādīnāṃ yajñīyānāṃ
vṛkṣāṇa meka syāvayabhūta gāīpatyasya paścime pradeśe upaviśya svayaṃ
kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratiṣajeta tṛṣṇa kṛṣṇamṛgasya carma kṛṣṇājinaṃ tat svayaṃ
skandhe pratiṣajeta adattamadhvaryuṇā etadādhvayevaṃ tadvacanāt svayaṃ
bhavatīti śradocitaḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratimuñceta iti tṛṣṇamiti mantre-
ādhastādgahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tasya pratiṣedhaḥ || 2 ||
paścimenāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramyaitat kuryāt | || 3 ||
kintu payādgārhapatyasyopaviśyeti yadukta tasyāyaṃ vikalpaḥ ||3||
hāhyāya netena sūtratrayaṃ kṛta tathā viśeṣatra kṛtaḥ |

śrautasūtre |
tasya tisriṣṭayaḥ pūrvāhna ekā pṛthak ca madhyandināparā-
hṛyoḥ * || 4 ||
tasya tila iṣṭayaḥ stomasaṃsthā vikṛtaṃ gavāmayanaṃ sarpasatraṃ syādi-

sarvo daśadaśīti stomo vikṛtaḥ agniṣṭomameva iti saṃsthā-
